# <a name="using-the-performance-analysis-of-logs-pal-tool"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-102">使用日志 (PAL) 工具的性能分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-102">Using the Performance Analysis of Logs (PAL) Tool</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-103">PAL （性能分析的日志） 工具读取性能监视器计数器日志 （任何已知格式） 中，并使用复杂，但已知阈值 （提供） 进行分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-103">The PAL (Performance Analysis of Logs) tool reads in a performance monitor counter log (any known format) and analyzes it using complex, but known thresholds (provided).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-104">该工具生成基于 HTML 报告，以图形方式图表重要的性能计数器，并引发警报时超出阈值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-104">The tool generates an HTML based report that graphically charts important performance counters and throws alerts when thresholds are exceeded.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-105">阈值最初根据阈值定义的 Microsoft 产品团队包括[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)]，和成员的 Microsoft 支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-105">The thresholds are originally based on thresholds defined by the Microsoft product teams, including [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)], and members of Microsoft support.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-106">此工具不是传统的性能分析的替代，但它可自动执行的性能计数器日志足够来帮助您节省大量时间的分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-106">This tool is not a replacement of traditional performance analysis, but it automates the analysis of performance counter logs enough to help save you time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-107">PAL 工具中：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-107">The PAL tool:</span></span>  
  
-   <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-108">分析阈值的性能计数器日志</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-108">Analyzes performance counter logs for thresholds</span></span>  
  
-   <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-109">适用于下列大型 Perfmon 日志</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-109">Is helpful for large Perfmon logs</span></span>  
  
-   <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-110">标识[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)]和通过分析阈值的操作系统性能计数器瓶颈</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-110">Identifies [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)] and operating system performance counter bottlenecks by analyzing for thresholds</span></span>  
  
-   <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-111">可以扩展以对任何性能计数器进行分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-111">Is extensible to do analysis on any performance counters</span></span>  
  
-   <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-112">可以用于帮助编写你自己的计数器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-112">Can be used to help write your own counter</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-113">PAL 是可用作在免费下载[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=98098](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=98098)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-113">PAL is available as a free download at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=98098](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=98098).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-114">它需要 Microsoft Log Parser。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-114">It requires Microsoft Log Parser.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-115">Log Parser 是一个功能强大、 通用的工具，如事件日志、 注册表、 文件系统和活动 Windows 操作系统上提供对基于文本的数据，例如日志文件、 XML 文件，CSV 文件，以及密钥的数据源的通用查询访问权限Directory® 目录服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-115">Log Parser is a powerful, versatile tool that provides universal query access to text-based data such as log files, XML files, and CSV files, as well as key data sources on the Windows operating system such as the event log, the registry, the file system, and Active Directory® directory service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-116">你可能想要使用此工具来查询占用大量的日志记录信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-116">You may want to use this tool to query a significant amount of logging information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-117">你可以下载的 Log Parser 工具在[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=85574](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=85574)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-117">You can download the Log Parser tool at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=85574](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=85574).</span></span>  
  
## <a name="using-pal-with-performance-counter-logs-in-different-languages"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-118">在不同语言中与性能计数器一起使用 PAL 日志</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-118">Using PAL with Performance Counter Logs in Different Languages</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-119">PAL 工具将分析仅在英语语言中的性能计数器日志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-119">The PAL tool analyzes performance counter logs only in English language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-120">若要使用其他语言中的性能计数器日志 PAL 工具，必须首先将日志传输到英语语言的转换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-120">To use the PAL tool with performance counter logs in other languages, you must first translate the logs to English language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-121">你可以使用**Perfmon 日志转换器**工具，可在[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=158802](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=158802)翻译为英语原始性能计数器日志文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-121">You can use the **Perfmon Log Translator** tool available at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=158802](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=158802) to translate the original performance counter log files to English.</span></span>  
  
## <a name="understanding-the-pal-tool-report-for-microsoft-biztalk-server-2010"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-122">了解 Microsoft BizTalk Server 2010 PAL 工具报告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-122">Understanding the PAL Tool Report for Microsoft BizTalk Server 2010</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-123">PAL 工具为 Windows 操作系统的 Microsoft SQL Server 提供 Perfmon 日志分析的阈值和[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-123">The PAL tool provides Perfmon log analysis of thresholds for the Windows operating system, Microsoft SQL Server, and [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)].</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-124">本部分介绍在分析的大多数[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]阈值 PAL 工具中的报表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-124">This section describes most of the analyses in the [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)] threshold report in the PAL tool.</span></span>  
  
> [!NOTE]  
>  <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-125">本主题是长，以便可以在一个位置以方便参考包含有关 PAL 工具的完整信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-125">This topic is long so that comprehensive information about the PAL tool can be contained in one place for easy reference.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-126">以下的分析和阈值由 PAL 工具进行报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-126">The following analysis and thresholds are reported by the PAL tool.</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-127">分析类型和名称</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-127">Analysis Type and Name</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-128">分析说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-128">Analysis Description</span></span>|  
|----------------------------|--------------------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-129">核心转储的磁盘： 磁盘可用空间</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-129">Disk: Disk Free Space for a Kernel Dump</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-130">此分析将检查以确保要转储到磁盘的所有内存的操作系统的可用磁盘空间不足。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-130">This analysis checks to make sure there is enough free disk space for the operating system to dump all memory to disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-131">如果可用磁盘空间不足，然后系统将无法创建 memory.dmp，即分析内核转储的根本原因所需的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-131">If insufficient disk space is available, then the operating system will fail to create a memory.dmp, file which is necessary to analyze the root cause of a kernel dump.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-132">磁盘： 逻辑/物理磁盘接口分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-132">Disk: Logical/Physical Disk Interface Analysis</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-133">此分析中查找的每个物理磁盘的空闲时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-133">This analysis looks at the idle time of each of the physical disks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-134">越空闲磁盘已，越低从中使用该磁盘。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-134">The more idle the disk is, the less the disk is being used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-135">在逻辑磁盘中使用一个磁盘时，最好使用此计数器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-135">This counter is best used when one disk is used in the logical disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-136">"%空闲时间"报告的示例间隔期间磁盘空闲时间百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-136">“% Idle Time” reports the percentage of time during the sample interval that the disk was idle.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-137">参考： 允许在磁盘密集型问题[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=50669](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=50669)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-137">Reference:  Ruling Out Disk-Bound Problems at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=50669](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=50669)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-138">磁盘： 逻辑/物理磁盘读取/写入延迟分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-138">Disk: Logical/Physical Disk Read/Write Latency Analysis</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-139">Windows 检测磁盘性能瓶颈的最可靠方法是通过测量其响应时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-139">The most reliable way for Windows to detect a disk performance bottleneck is by measuring its response times.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-140">如果响应时间大于.025 （25 毫秒为单位），就是一个保守的阈值，然后可能发生明显减慢速度和影响用户的性能问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-140">If the response times are greater than .025 (25 milliseconds), which is a conservative threshold, then noticeable slow-downs and performance issues affecting users may be occurring.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-141">详细信息，请参阅本主题中的逻辑/物理磁盘读取/写入延迟分析到。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-141">For more information, refer to Logical/Physical Disk Read/Write Latency Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-142">磁盘： 逻辑磁盘传输次数/秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-142">Disk: Logical Disk Transfers/sec</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-143">"Disk Transfers/sec"是读取的速率和写入磁盘上的操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-143">“Disk Transfers/sec” is the rate of read and write operations on the disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-144">此分析检查以查看是否有任何逻辑磁盘的阈值展示较差的响应时间 （大于 25 秒 I/O 操作的响应时间）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-144">The thresholds for this analysis check to see whether any of the logical disks are showing poor response times (greater than 25 ms response times for I/O operations).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-145">如果是这样，每秒磁盘传输应在或更高版本 80。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-145">If this is true, then the disk transfers per second should be at or above 80.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-146">如果没有，则磁盘体系结构需要进行调查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-146">If not, then the disk architecture needs to be investigated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-147">不佳的磁盘 I/O 的最常见原因是重载 SAN 上的 LUN。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-147">The most common cause of poor disk I/O is LUN overloading on the SAN.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-148">有关详细信息，请参阅本主题中的逻辑 Disk Transfers/sec。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-148">For more information, refer to Logical Disk Transfers/sec in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-149">磁盘： 逻辑磁盘可用空间百分比</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-149">Disk: LogicalDisk % Free Space</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-150">"%可用空间"是已在所选逻辑磁盘驱动器上可用的总可用空间的百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-150">“% Free Space” is the percentage of total usable space that was free on the selected logical disk drive.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-151">小于 30%的可用磁盘驱动器空间之前，应不会影响性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-151">Performance should not be affected until the available disk drive space is less than 30 percent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-152">当使用磁盘驱动器的 70%时，剩余的可用空间位于更靠近到磁盘的主轴，在磁盘驱动器，在较低的性能级别运行的中心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-152">When 70 percent of the disk drive is used, the remaining free space is located closer to the disk's spindle at the center of the disk drive, which operates at a lower performance level.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-153">可用磁盘空间不足可能导致严重磁盘性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-153">Lack of free disk space can cause severe disk performance.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-154">参考： NT 服务器和磁盘子系统性能在[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106783](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106783)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-154">Reference:  NT Server and Disk Subsystem Performance at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106783](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106783)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-155">磁盘： 处理 IO Data Operations/sec 和处理 IO 其他操作数/秒分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-155">Disk: Process IO Data Operations/sec and Process IO Other Operations/sec Analysis</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-156">这些计数器计数生成的包括文件、 网络和设备 I/o 的过程的所有 I/O 活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-156">These counters count all I/O activity generated by the process to include file, network and device I/Os.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-157">进程正在 1,000 多个我 / O 每秒的并将其标记为警告时，将检查这些分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-157">These analyses check when processes are doing more than 1,000 I/O’s per second and flag it as a warning.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-158">这些分析最与其他分析 （如磁盘分析） 相关联时用于确定哪些进程可能会涉及到的 I/O 活动中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-158">These analyses are best used in correlation with other analyses such as disk analysis to determine which processes might be involved in the I/O activity.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-159">内存： 可用内存</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-159">Memory: Available Memory</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-160">此分析检查的总的可用内存是否不足 – 10%可用处出现警告和在 5%可用的关键。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-160">This analysis checks whether the total available memory is low – Warning at 10 percent available and Critical at 5 percent available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-161">下降趋势的 10 MB 的每小时检测到时，并可表示潜在的即将到来的内存不足情况，警告也会得到通知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-161">A warning is also alerted when a decreasing trend of 10 MB’s per hour is detected, which can indicate a potential upcoming memory condition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-162">物理内存不足可能导致增加特权模式下 CPU 和系统延迟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-162">Low physical memory can cause increased privileged mode CPU and system delays.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-163">详细信息，请参阅本主题中的可用 MemoryAnalysis 到。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-163">For more information, refer to Available MemoryAnalysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-164">内存： 可用系统页表项</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-164">Memory: Free System Page Table Entries</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-165">可用系统页表项 (PTE) 是当前未使用的系统页表条目数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-165">Free System Page Table Entries (PTE’s) are the number of page table entries not currently used by the system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-166">此分析将决定是否系统用完 PTE 的通过检查是否有少于 5000 免费 PTE 的伴有警告是否少于 10,000 免费 PTE 的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-166">This analysis determines whether the system is running out of PTE’s by checking whether there are fewer than 5,000 free PTE’s with a Warning if there are fewer than 10,000 free PTE’s.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-167">缺乏足够 PTE 可能会导致系统范围内挂起。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-167">Lack of enough PTE’s can result in systemwide hangs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-168">此外请注意，3 GB 切换将大幅降低免费 PTE 的量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-168">Also note that the /3GB switch will lower the amount of free PTE’s significantly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-169">详细信息，请参阅本主题中的可用系统页表条目分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-169">For more information, refer to Free System Page Table Entries Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-170">内存： 内存泄漏检测</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-170">Memory: Memory Leak Detection</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-171">此分析将决定是否任何进程正在消耗大量的系统的内存，且是否在内存消耗，随着时间的推移增加过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-171">This analysis determines whether any of the processes are consuming a large amount of the system's memory and whether the process is increasing in memory consumption over time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-172">使用大量的内存的进程没什么，只要该过程将返回到系统内存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-172">A process consuming large portions of memory is fine as long as the process returns the memory back to the system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-173">查找增加图表的趋势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-173">Look for increasing trends in the chart.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-174">上升趋势长的一段时间内无法指示内存泄漏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-174">An increasing trend over a long period of time could indicate a memory leak.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-175">"Private Bytes"是内存的当前大小 （字节），此进程已分配不能与其他进程共享。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-175">“Private Bytes” is the current size, in bytes, of memory that this process has allocated that cannot be shared with other processes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-176">此分析检查 10 MB 的每小时和 5 MB 的每小时增加趋势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-176">This analysis checks for 10 MB’s per hour and 5 MB’s per hour increasing trends.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-177">与 PAL 中的可用内存分析相关联时使用此分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-177">Use this analysis in correlation with the Available Memory analysis in PAL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-178">详细信息，请参阅本主题中的内存泄漏检测分析到。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-178">For more information, refer to Memory Leak Detection Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-179">内存： 句柄泄漏检测</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-179">Memory: Handle Leak Detection</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-180">此分析检查的所有进程以确定多少处理每个已打开，以确定是否可以句柄泄漏怀疑不当。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-180">This analysis checks all of the processes to determine how many handles each has open and to determine whether a handle leak is suspected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-181">具有大量的句柄和/或主动上升趋势的进程可能表示句柄泄漏，这通常会导致内存泄漏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-181">A process with a large number of handles and/or an aggressive upward trend could indicate a handle leak, which typically results in a memory leak.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-182">此进程当前打开的句柄的总数等于此进程中的每个线程当前打开的句柄总数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-182">The total number of handles currently open by this process is equal to the sum of the handles currently open by each thread in this process.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-183">参考： 调试诊断工具 v1.1 在[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106784](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106784)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-183">Reference:  Debug Diagnostic Tool v1.1 at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106784](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106784)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-184">内存： 内存 Pages Input/sec</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-184">Memory: Memory Pages Input/sec</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-185">"页 Input/sec"是从磁盘为解决强制分页错误读取页的速率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-185">“Pages Input/sec” is the rate at which pages are read from disk to resolve hard page faults.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-186">如果进程引用不在其工作集或其他位置在物理内存中，并且必须从磁盘检索的虚拟内存中的页，将发生硬页面错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-186">Hard page faults occur when a process refers to a page in virtual memory that is not in its working set or elsewhere in physical memory, and must be retrieved from disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-187">此分析将检查是否有 10 个以上页文件的读取次数 / 秒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-187">This analysis checks whether there are more than 10 page file reads per second.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-188">内存： 内存页/秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-188">Memory: Memory Pages/sec</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-189">此分析检查"页/秒"是否为高 （超过 1,000 个）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-189">This analysis checks to see whether the “Pages/sec” is high (above 1,000).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-190">如果高，然后系统可能内存不足尝试进行分页到磁盘的内存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-190">If it is high, then the system is likely running out of memory by trying to page the memory to the disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-191">"页/秒"是从读取或写入磁盘为解决强制分页错误页的速率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-191">“Pages/sec” is the rate at which pages are read from or written to disk to resolve hard page faults.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-192">此计数器是导致系统范围延迟的错误种类的主要指示器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-192">This counter is a primary indicator of the kinds of faults that cause systemwide delays.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-193">可用内存分析和 PAL 中的内存泄漏检测分析与相关联时使用此分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-193">Use this analysis in correlation with Available Memory analysis and Memory Leak Detection analysis in PAL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-194">如果所有这些分析在同一时间引发警报，，这可能表示系统内存不足和可疑的进程涉及和执行分析 PAL 中的内存泄漏检测分析中所述的步骤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-194">If all of these analyses are throwing alerts at the same time, then this may indicate the system is running out of memory and the suspected processes involved and follow analysis steps mentioned in the Memory Leak Detection analysis in PAL.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-195">有关详细信息，请参阅本主题中的内存页/秒分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-195">For more information, refer to Memory Pages/sec Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-196">内存： 内存系统缓存驻留字节数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-196">Memory: Memory System Cache Resident Bytes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-197">"系统缓存驻留字节数"是的大小，以字节为单位，在文件系统缓存中的可分页操作系统代码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-197">“System Cache Resident Bytes” is the size, in bytes, of the pageable operating system code in the file system cache.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-198">此值只包括当前物理页面，并且不包括任何当前未驻留的虚拟内存页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-198">This value includes only current physical pages and does not include any virtual memory pages not currently resident.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-199">此值是一个组件的"内存\\\System 代码驻留字节数"表示所有当前正在物理内存的可分页操作系统代码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-199">This value is a component of “Memory\\\System Code Resident Bytes” which represents all pageable operating system code that is currently in physical memory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-200">此计数器显示上次观测的值仅;它不是平均值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-200">This counter displays the last observed value only; it is not an average.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-201">此分析检查上升趋势的 10 MB 的每小时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-201">This analysis checks for an increasing trend of 10 MB’s per hour.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-202">承受负载时，服务器可能使用的系统缓存，以便缓存如磁盘 I/O 活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-202">Under load, a server might use the system cache in order to cache I/O activity such as disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-203">将相关联时使用与过程 IO Data Operations/sec 和进程 IO 其他操作数/秒 PAL 中的分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-203">Use in correlation with Process IO Data Operations/sec and Process IO Other Operations/sec analyses in PAL.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-204">参考： 文件缓存性能和优化在[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106786](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106786)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-204">Reference: File Cache Performance and Tuning at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106786](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106786)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-205">内存： 池非分页字节数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-205">Memory: Pool Non Paged Bytes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-206">"池非分页字节数"是的大小，以字节为单位，无法写入到的对象的系统内存区域的非分页池的磁盘、 但一旦分配就必须保留在物理内存中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-206">“Pool Nonpaged Bytes” is the size, in bytes, of the non-paged pool, an area of system memory for objects that cannot be written to disk, but must remain in physical memory as long as they are allocated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-207">此分析将检查以查看是否系统即将接近最大池非分页内存大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-207">This analysis checks to see whether the system is coming close to the maximum pool non paged memory size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-208">这是通过估计考虑到的池大小/3 GB、 物理内存大小和 32 位/64 位，然后确定的值是否高于 60%的估计的池大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-208">It does this by estimating the pool sizes taking into consideration /3GB, physical memory size, and 32-bit/64-bit, then determining whether the value is higher than 60 percent of the estimated pool size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-209">如果系统变得接近最大大小时，然后系统可能会遇到系统宽挂起。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-209">If the system becomes close to the maximum size, then the system could experience system wide hangs.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-210">Boot.ini 文件中的 3 GB 交换机选项大大降低了此内存池的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-210">The /3GB switch option in the boot.ini file significantly reduces the size of this memory pool.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-211">详细信息，请参阅本主题中的 Pool Non-Paged 字节分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-211">For more information, refer to Pool Non-Paged Bytes Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-212">内存： 池分页字节数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-212">Memory: Pool Paged Bytes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-213">此分析将检查以查看是否系统即将接近最大池分页内存大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-213">This analysis checks to see whether the system is coming close to the maximum pool paged memory size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-214">这是通过估计考虑到的池大小/3 GB、 物理内存大小和 32 位/64 位，然后确定的值是否高于 60%的估计的池大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-214">It does this by estimating the pool sizes taking into consideration /3GB, physical memory size, and 32-bit/64-bit, then determining whether the value is higher than 60 percent of the estimated pool size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-215">如果系统变得接近最大大小时，然后系统可能会遇到系统宽挂起。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-215">If the system becomes close to the maximum size, then the system could experience system wide hangs.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-216">Boot.ini 文件中的 3 GB 交换机选项大大降低了此内存池的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-216">The /3GB switch option in the boot.ini file significantly reduces the size of this memory pool.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-217">详细信息，请参阅本主题中的池分页字节分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-217">For more information, refer to Pool Paged Bytes Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-218">内存： 进程线程计数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-218">Memory: Process Thread Count</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-219">此分析检查的所有进程来确定进程是否具有 500 多个线程，且由每小时 50 线程如果增加线程数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-219">This analysis checks all of the processes to determine whether a process has more than 500 threads and if the number of threads is increasing by 50 threads per hour.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-220">具有大量的线程和/或主动上升趋势的进程无法指示线程泄漏这通常会导致内存泄漏或高上下文切换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-220">A process with a large number of threads and/or an aggressive upward trend could indicate a thread leak which typically results in either a memory leak or high context switching.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-221">高上下文切换将导致高特权模式下 CPU。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-221">High context switching will result in high privileged mode CPU.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-222">内存： 进程工作集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-222">Memory: Process Working Set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-223">"工作集"是当前大小 （字节），此过程的工作集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-223">“Working Set” is the current size, in bytes, of the working set of this process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-224">工作集是的进程中的线程最近使用过的内存页的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-224">The working set is the set of memory pages touched recently by the threads in the process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-225">如果计算机中的可用内存高于阈值，页会保留在某一进程工作集，即使它们未被使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-225">If free memory in the computer is above a threshold, pages are left in the working set of a process even if they are not in use.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-226">如果可用内存降到阈值以下，将从工作集中削减页。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-226">When free memory falls below a threshold, pages are trimmed from working sets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-227">如果需要它们将会软恢复到的工作集在离开主内存之前。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-227">If they are needed they will then be soft-faulted back into the working set before leaving main memory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-228">此分析检查的 10 MB 上升趋势达到或超过每个进程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-228">This analysis checks for an increasing trend of 10 MB’s or more in each of the processes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-229">PAL 中的可用内存分析的使用相关联时使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-229">Use in correlation with Available Memory analysis in PAL.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-230">参考： 检测在内存瓶颈[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106787](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106787)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-230">Reference:  Detecting Memory Bottlenecks at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106787](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106787)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-231">网络： 网络输出队列长度分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-231">Network: Network Output Queue Length Analysis</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-232">此分析检查多少线程在等待网络适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-232">This analysis checks to see how many threads are waiting on the network adapter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-233">如果多个线程在等待上的网络适配器，然后系统可能占满网络 I/O 由于网络滞后或网络带宽。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-233">If a lot of threads are waiting on the network adapter, then the system is probably saturating the network I/O due to network latency or network bandwidth.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-234">"Output Queue Length"是 （以数据包） 的输出数据包队列的长度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-234">“Output Queue Length” is the length of the output packet queue (in packets).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-235">指示延迟如果这是长度大于 2，和瓶颈应找出并消除，如有可能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-235">Delays are indicated if this is longer than two, and the bottleneck should be found and eliminated, if possible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-236">网络输出队列的典型原因包括大量的小型网络请求和网络延迟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-236">Typical causes of network output queuing include high numbers of small network requests and network latency.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-237">网络： 网络使用率分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-237">Network: Network Utilization Analysis</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-238">"Bytes Total/sec"是发送和接收每个网络适配器，包括组帧字符字节的速率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-238">“Bytes Total/sec” is the rate at which bytes are sent and received over each network adapter, including framing characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-239">"Network Interface\Bytes Received/sec"是"Network Interface\Bytes Received/sec"和"Network Interface\Bytes Sent/sec"的和。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-239">“Network Interface\Bytes Received/sec” is a sum of “Network Interface\Bytes Received/sec” and “Network Interface\Bytes Sent/sec”.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-240">此计数器可帮助你知道在你的网络适配器的流量是否已饱和以及是否需要添加另一个网络适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-240">This counter helps you know whether the traffic at your network adapter is saturated and whether you need to add another network adapter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-241">可以确定问题的速度取决于类型的网络必须以及是否与其他应用程序共享带宽。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-241">How quickly you can identify a problem depends on the type of network you have as well as whether you share bandwidth with other applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-242">此分析将"Bytes Total/sec"转换为位，并将它与计算网络利用率的网络适配器的当前带宽进行比较。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-242">This analysis converts “Bytes Total/sec” to bits and compares it to the current bandwidth of the network adapter to calculate network utilization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-243">接下来，它会检查 50%以上的使用率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-243">Next, it checks for utilization above 50 percent.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-244">参考： 测量在.NET 应用程序性能[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106788](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106788)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-244">Reference:  Measuring .NET Application Performance at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106788](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106788)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-245">分页文件： 分页文件使用率 %和 %使用高峰</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-245">Paging File: Paging File % Usage and % Usage Peak</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-246">在 %中使用的页文件实例的量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-246">The amount of the page file instance in use in percent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-247">另请参阅"过程\\\Page 文件字节数"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-247">See also “Process\\\Page File Bytes”.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-248">此分析检查是否大于 70%的使用率的百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-248">This analysis checks whether the percentage of usage is greater than 70 percent.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-249">处理器： 处理器使用率分析和进程的过多的处理器使用率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-249">Processor: Processor Utilization Analysis and Excessive Processor Use by Processes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-250">此计数器是处理器活动的主要指示器，并显示在采样间隔期间观察到的忙碌时间的平均百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-250">This counter is the primary indicator of processor activity and displays the average percentage of busy time observed during the sample interval.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-251">它被通过监视服务处于非活动状态的时间，然后从 100%减去该值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-251">It is calculated by monitoring the time that the service is inactive and subtracting that value from 100 percent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-252">此分析检查大于每个处理器上的 60%的利用率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-252">This analysis checks for utilization greater than 60 percent on each processor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-253">如果是这样，确定它是否是高用户模式 CPU 或高特权模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-253">If so, determine whether it is high user mode CPU or high privileged mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-254">如果高特权模式下 CPU 怀疑有问题，请参阅 PAL 中的特权模式 CPU 分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-254">If high privileged mode CPU is suspected, then see the Privileged Mode CPU analysis in PAL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-255">如果怀疑用户模式下处理器瓶颈，则可以考虑使用进程探查器分析导致高 CPU 使用的函数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-255">If a user-mode processor bottleneck is suspected, then consider using a process profiler to analyze the functions causing the high CPU consumption.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-256">处理器： 处理器队列长度</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-256">Processor: Processor Queue Length</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-257">此分析将决定是否平均处理器队列长度超过处理器的数目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-257">This analysis determines whether the average processor queue length exceeds the number of processors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-258">如果是这样，则这可能表示处理器瓶颈。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-258">If so, then this could indicate a processor bottleneck.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-259">通过 PAL 中的过程分析特权模式 CPU 分析和过多的处理器使用的相关中使用此分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-259">Use this analysis in correlation with Privileged Mode CPU analysis and Excessive Processor Use by Process analysis in PAL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-260">详细信息，请参阅本主题中的处理器队列长度分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-260">For detailed information, refer to Processor Queue Length Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-261">处理器： 特权模式下 CPU 分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-261">Processor:  Privileged Mode CPU Analysis</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-262">此计数器指示在特权模式下运行的线程的时间的百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-262">This counter indicates the percentage of time a thread runs in privileged mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-263">当你的应用程序调用时 （例如，可执行文件或网络 I/O 或分配内存） 的操作系统功能时，这些操作系统功能在特权模式下执行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-263">When your application calls operating system functions (for example to perform file or network I/O or to allocate memory), these operating system functions are executed in privileged mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-264">此分析将检查以查看特权模式下 CPU 是否占用了超过 30%的总 CPU。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-264">This analysis checks to see whether privileged mode CPU is consuming more than 30 percent of total CPU.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-265">如果这样，则可能的 CPU 消耗是才导致的网络、 内存或磁盘 I/O 等处理器以外的另一个瓶颈。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-265">If so, then the CPU consumption is likely caused by another bottleneck other than the processor such as network, memory, or disk I/O.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-266">与处理器相关联时使用: %Interrupt Time 和处理器： PAL 中的高上下文切换分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-266">Use in correlation with Processor:  % Interrupt Time and Processor:  High Context Switching analyses in PAL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-267">详细信息，请参阅本主题中的特权模式 CPU 分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-267">For more information, refer to Privileged Mode CPU Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-268">处理器： 中断时间</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-268">Processor: Interrupt Time</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-269">"%中断时间"是处理器用于接收和服务硬件中断采样间隔期间的时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-269">“% Interrupt Time” is the time the processor spends receiving and servicing hardware interrupts during sample intervals.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-270">此值是活动的生成中断，例如系统时钟、 鼠标、 磁盘驱动程序、 数据通讯线路、 网络接口卡和其他外围设备的设备的间接指示器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-270">This value is an indirect indicator of the activity of devices that generate interrupts, such as the system clock, the mouse, disk drivers, data communication lines, network interface cards and other peripheral devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-271">这些设备通常会中断处理器，在已经完成了任务或需要关注时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-271">These devices normally interrupt the processor when they have completed a task or require attention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-272">中断期间是暂挂正常线程执行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-272">Normal thread execution is suspended during interrupts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-273">大多数系统时钟每隔 10 毫秒，创建中断活动的背景就会中断处理器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-273">Most system clocks interrupt the processor every 10 milliseconds, creating a background of interrupt activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-274">大幅度提高此计数器指示潜在硬件问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-274">A dramatic increase in this counter indicates potential hardware problems.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-275">此分析检查"%中断时间"大于 30%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-275">This analysis checks for “% Interrupt Time” greater than 30 percent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-276">如果发生这种情况，请考虑更新与此警报关联的硬件的设备驱动程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-276">If this occurs, then consider updating devices drivers for hardware that correlates to this alert.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-277">参考： 测量在.NET 应用程序性能[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106788](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106788)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-277">Reference: Measuring .NET Application Performance at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106788](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106788)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-278">处理器： 高上下文切换</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-278">Processor:  High Context Switching</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-279">较高优先级的线程会抢占较低的优先级线程当前正在运行或高优先级的线程块时，会发生情况的上下文切换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-279">A context switch happens when a higher priority thread preempts a lower priority thread that is currently running or when a high priority thread blocks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-280">当多个线程共享相同的优先级级别，则会发生的上下文切换的高级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-280">High levels of context switching can occur when many threads share the same priority level.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-281">这通常指示线程过多在争夺系统上的处理器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-281">This often indicates that too many threads are competing for the processors on the system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-282">一般情况下，上下文切换速率小于每个处理器每秒 5,000 的不是值得担心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-282">As a general rule, context switching rates of less than 5,000 per second per processor are not worth worrying about.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-283">如果上下文切换率超过每个处理器每秒的 15000，则一个约束。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-283">If context switching rates exceed 15,000 per second per processor, then there is a constraint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-284">详细信息，请参阅本主题中的高上下文切换分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-284">For more information, refer to High Context Switching Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-285">Microsof [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]: BizTalk 冻结过程中业务流程</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-285">Microsof [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]: BizTalk Dehydrating Orchestrations</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-286">当同时运行多长时间运行的业务流程时，可能会出现内存和性能问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-286">When many long-running business processes are running at the same time, memory and performance issues are possible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-287">业务流程引擎通过“冻结”和“解除冻结”业务流程实例来解决这些问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-287">The orchestration engine addresses these issues by "dehydrating" and "rehydrating" orchestration instances.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-288">冻结是将业务流程的状态序列化到 SQL Server 数据库中的过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-288">Dehydration is the process of serializing the state of an orchestration into a SQL Server database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-289">Rehydration 是此过程的反向： 反序列化从数据库的业务流程的上次运行状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-289">Rehydration is the reverse of this process: deserializing the last running state of an orchestration from the database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-290">冻结用于通过减少必须在内存中同时实例化的业务流程数来最大程度地降低系统资源的使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-290">Dehydration is used to minimize the use of system resources by reducing the number of orchestrations that have to be instantiated in memory at one time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-291">因此，dehyrations 节省内存消耗，但代价相对较大要执行的操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-291">Therefore, dehyrations save memory consumption, but are relatively expensive operations to perform.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-292">此分析检查 dehydrations 10 或更多。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-292">This analysis checks for dehydrations of 10 or more.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-293">如果是这样，[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)]可能内存不足 （虚拟或物理），较高的业务流程数在等待消息，或未正确设置冻结设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-293">If so, [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)] may be running out of memory (either virtual or physical), a high number of orchestrations are waiting on messages, or the dehydration settings are not set properly.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-294">参考： Orchestration 冻结和在 Rehydration [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155284](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155284)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-294">Reference:  Orchestration Dehydration and Rehydration at  [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155284](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155284)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-295">Microsoft [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]: BizTalk 高数据库会话</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-295">Microsoft [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]:  BizTalk High Database Sessions</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-296">此计数器都有两个可能值： 正常 (0) 或超出了阈值 (1)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-296">This counter has two possible values: normal (0) or exceeded (1).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-297">此分析检查的值为 1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-297">This analysis checks for a value of 1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-298">如果是这样，BizTalk 超过了允许的数据库会话数的阈值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-298">If so, BizTalk has exceeded the threshold of the number of database sessions permitted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-299">此值由 BizTalk 主机限制设置中的"每个 CPU 的数据库连接"值控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-299">This value is controlled by the “Database connection per CPU” value in the BizTalk Host Throttling settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-300">"数据库连接每个 CPU"是最大并发数据库会话数 （每个 CPU) 限制开始之前允许。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-300">“Database connection per CPU” is the maximum number of concurrent database sessions (per CPU) allowed before throttling begins.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-301">通过使用 BizTalk:Message Agent 性能对象类别下的 Database session BizTalk:Message Agent performance object category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-302">此参数只影响出站消息阻止功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-302">This parameter only affects outbound message throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-303">有关详细信息，请参考 BizTalk 高数据库会话分析中本主题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-303">For more information, refer to |<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-304">Microsoft [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]: BizTalk 高数据库大小</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-304">Microsoft [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]: BizTalk High Database Size</span></span>|<span the message count in database threshold occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-306">默认情况下，主机消息限制阈值的数据库中的计数设置为值为 50000，就会触发在下列情况下的限制条件：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-306">By default the host message count in database throttling threshold is set to a value of 50,000, which will trigger a throttling condition under the following 消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-308">-   The number of messages in the spool table or the tracking table exceeds 500,000 messages.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-309">如果发生这种情况，请考虑将减少在数据库中的消息数的操作过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-309">If this occurs, then consider a course of action that will reduce the number of class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-310">For example, ensure the SQL Server jobs in [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)] are running without error and use the Group Hub page in the [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)] Administration console to determine whether message build up is caused by large numbers of suspended messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-311">有关详细信息，请参考 BizTalk 高数据库大小分析中本主题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-311">For more information, refer to BizTalk High Database Size Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-312">Microsoft [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]: BizTalk 高进程内消息计数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-312">Microsoft [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]:  BizTalk High In-Process Message Count</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-313">此分析检查的进程内消息计数高计数器以确定是否发生这种类型的限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-313">This analysis checks the High In-Process Message Count counter to determine whether this kind of throttling is occurring.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-314">如果是这样，请考虑调整"每 CPU 邮件进程内"设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-314">If so, consider adjusting the “In-Process messages per CPU” setting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-315">此参数只影响出站消息阻止功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-315">This parameter only affects outbound message throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-316">在禁用限制基于每个 CPU 进程内消息数"进程内消息每个 CPU"设置中输入的值为 0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-316">Enter a value of 0 in the “In-Process messages per CPU” setting to disable throttling based on the number of in-process messages per CPU.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-317">"进程内消息每个 CPU"设置的默认值为 1000。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-317">The default value for the “In-Process messages per CPU” setting is 1,000.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-318">请注意，修改此值还可以影响在低延迟的消息和/或 BizTalk 资源的效率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-318">Note that modifying this value can also have an impact on low latency of messages and/or the efficiency of BizTalk resources.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-319">详细信息，请参阅本主题中的 BizTalk 高进程内消息计数分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-319">For more information, refer to BizTalk High In-Process Message Count Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-344">Microsoft [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]: BizTalk 高线程计数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-344">Microsoft [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]:  BizTalk High Thread Count</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-345">"每个 CPU 线程数"是宿主进程包括由适配器使用的线程中的线程总数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-345">“Threads Per CPU” is the total number of threads in the host process including threads used by adapters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-346">如果超出此阈值，[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)]将尝试减小 EPM 线程池和消息代理线程池的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-346">If this threshold is exceeded, [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)] will try to reduce the size of the EPM thread pool and message agent thread pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-347">如果高负载可能导致创建大量线程，则在这种情况下，应启用基于线程的阻止功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-347">Thread based throttling should be enabled in scenarios where high load can lead to the creation of a large number of threads.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-348">此参数同时影响入站和出站阻止功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-348">This parameter affects both inbound and outbound throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-349">默认情况下，禁用基于线程限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-349">Thread based throttling is disabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-350">详细信息，请参阅本主题中的 BizTalk 高线程计数分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-350">For more information, refer to BizTalk High Thread Count Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-359">Microsoft [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]: BizTalk 主机挂起消息队列长度</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-359">Microsoft [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]: BizTalk Host Suspended Messages Queue Length</span></span>|<span host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-361">将挂起的消息是消息或业务流程的一个实例，[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)]已停止处理因出错而系统或消息中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-361">A suspended message is an instance of a message or orchestration that [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)] has stopped processing due to an error in the system or the message.</span></span> <span resolution of the system issue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-363">通常情况下，由于消息问题而挂起的实例不是可恢复，并且必须修复和重新提交到消息本身[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)]系统。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-363">Often, suspended instances due to a message problem are not resumable, and the message itself must be fixed and resubmitted to the [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)] system.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-364">挂起的消息队列是一个包含工作项，为其错误或失败期间遇到处理的队列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-364">The suspended message queue is a queue that contains work items for which an error or failure was encountered during processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-365">挂起队列将一直存储这些消息，直到它们被纠正、重新处理或被删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-365">A suspended queue stores the messages until they can be corrected and reprocessed, or deleted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-366">此分析检查挂起的任何的消息匹配项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-366">This analysis checks for any occurrence of suspended messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-367">上升趋势可能表示严重处理错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-367">An increasing trend could indicate severe processing errors.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-368">参考： BizTalk Server 2004： 监视和故障排除在[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108771](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108771)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-368">Reference:  BizTalk Server 2004: Monitoring and Troubleshooting at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108771](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108771)</span></span>|  
|[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-369">: BizTalk 空闲业务流程</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-369">:  BizTalk Idle Orchestrations</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-370">当前以主机实例为宿主的空闲业务流程实例的数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-370">Number of idle orchestration instances currently hosted by the host instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-371">此计数器是指业务流程，不需要进度但不是可冻结。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-371">This counter refers to orchestrations that are not making progress but are not dehydratable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-372">业务流程被阻止时，发生这种情况，可以等待接收，侦听或原子事务的延迟时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-372">This situation can occur when the orchestration is blocked, waiting for a receive, listen, or delay in an atomic transaction.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-373">如果大量的非可冻结业务流程会累积，BizTalk 可能用尽内存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-373">If a large number of non-dehydratable orchestrations accumulate, then BizTalk may run out of memory.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-374">冻结是将业务流程的状态序列化到 SQL Server 数据库中的过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-374">Dehydration is the process of serializing the state of an orchestration into a SQL Server database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-375">Rehydration 是此过程的反向： 反序列化从数据库的业务流程的上次运行状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-375">Rehydration is the reverse of this process: deserializing the last running state of an orchestration from the database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-376">冻结用于通过减少必须在内存中同时实例化的业务流程数来最大程度地降低系统资源的使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-376">Dehydration is used to minimize the use of system resources by reducing the number of orchestrations that have to be instantiated in memory at one time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-377">引擎 dehydrates 实例的保存状态，并释放的实例所需的内存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-377">The engine dehydrates the instance by saving the state, and frees up the memory required by the instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-378">通过冻结休眠业务流程实例过程中，引擎使大量的长时间运行业务流程，以同时在同一台计算机上运行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-378">By dehydrating dormant orchestration instances, the engine makes it possible for a large number of long-running business processes to run concurrently on the same computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-379">此分析检查每小时一个空闲的业务流程的上升趋势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-379">This analysis checks for an increasing trend of one idle [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155284](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155284)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-380">Reference: Orchestration Dehydration and |[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-385">: BizTalk 消息传递延迟</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-385">:  BizTalk Message Delivery Delay</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-386">这是对每个消息传递批处理 （如果要中止消息传递时适用） 的当前延迟以毫秒 (ms) 为单位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-386">This is the current delay in milliseconds (ms) imposed on each message delivery batch (applicable if the message delivery is being throttled).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-387">有关限制，延迟应用中发布或处理消息，具体取决于消息是入站或出站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-387">In regards to throttling, a delay is applied in the publishing or processing of the message, depending on whether the message is inbound or outbound.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-388">延迟期成正比的重要程度限制条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-388">The delay period is proportional to the severity of the throttling condition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-389">限制条件的更高严重性将启动比限制条件的低严重性再限制期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-389">Higher severity throttling conditions will initiate a longer throttling period than lower severity throttling conditions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-390">随着阻止条件的变化，将根据阻止机制在特定范围内延长和缩短此延迟时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-390">This delay period is adjusted up and down within certain ranges by the throttling mechanism as conditions change.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-391">通过消息传递的延迟 (ms) 和消息发布与 BizTalk:Message 代理性能对象类别关联的延迟 (ms) 性能计数器公开当前延迟期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span performance object category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-392">此分析检查消息传递延迟大于 5 秒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-392">This analysis checks for a message delivery |[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-440">: BizTalk 业务流程丢弃</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-440">:  BizTalk Orchestrations Discarded</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-441">自从主机实例启动以来，内存中被丢弃的业务流程实例的数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-441">Number of orchestration instances discarded from memory since the host instance started.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-442">如果引擎未能持久化某个业务流程的状态，则会将其丢弃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-442">An orchestration can be discarded if the engine fails to persist its state.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-443">此分析将检查有任何丢弃消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-443">This analysis checks for any discarded messages.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-444">参考： BizTalk 核心引擎博客</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-444">Reference:  BizTalk Core Engine's WebLog</span></span><br />[<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-445">http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108775</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-445">http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108775</span></span>](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108775)|  
|[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-446">: BizTalk 业务流程驻留在内存中</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-446">:  BizTalk Orchestrations Resident in Memory</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-447">当前以主机实例为宿主的业务流程实例的数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-447">Number of orchestration instances currently hosted by the host instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-448">此分析检查在驻留在内存和是否超过 50%的驻留在内存中的业务流程不是可冻结业务流程中上升趋势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-448">This analysis checks for an increasing trend in orchestrations resident in memory and whether more than 50 percent of the orchestrations resident in memory are not dehydratable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-449">有关详细信息，请参阅 BizTalk 业务流程驻留在内存分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-449">For more information, refer to BizTalk Orchestrations Resident in Memory Analysis.</span></span>|

|[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-461">: 挂起消息 BizTalk</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-461">:  BizTalk Pending Messages</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-462">接收到 MessageBox 接收到未被确认的消息数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-462">The number of received messages that have not been acknowledged as received to the MessageBox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-463">挂起的消息的消息，已拉入内存传递到 XLANG 业务流程，但尚未被处理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-463">Pending messages are messages that have been pulled into memory and delivered to the XLANG orchestration, but have not yet been processed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-464">没有任何这种情况下如何处理数据丢失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-464">This circumstance has nothing to do with data loss.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-465">将一条消息传送到业务流程是一个多步骤过程，只需驻留在数据库中的假脱机表中的消息的实例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-465">Delivering a message to an orchestration is a multi-step process and is simply an instance of the message residing in the spool table in the database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-466">这些挂起消息计数为处理这些消息;因此，具有大量它们在内存中，这种情况可能会导致内存限制系统上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-466">These pending messages count as in-process messages; therefore, having a large number of them in memory could cause memory throttling on the system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-467">调整的内部消息队列大小设置无法帮助控制的挂起消息数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-467">Adjusting the Internal Message Queue Size setting could help with controlling the number of pending messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-468">每个 CPU 进程内消息设置产生影响限制将时调用了大量的挂起消息发生时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-468">The In-Process Messages Per CPU setting has an impact on when throttling will invoke when a high number of pending messages occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-469">这些设置位于 BizTalk 管理控制台中的主机属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-469">These setting are found in the Host properties in the BizTalk Administration Console.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-470">此分析检查此计数器仅显示统计。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-470">This analysis checks only shows statistics for this counter.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-471">参考： 业务流程引擎性能计数器在[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155290](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155290)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-471">Reference: Orchestration Engine Performance Counters at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155290](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155290)</span></span>|  
|[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-472">： BizTalk 持久性点每秒数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-472">:  BizTalk Persistence Points/second</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-473">平均每秒持久化业务流程实例的次数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-473">Average number of orchestration instances persisted per second.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-474">业务流程引擎保存在不同的时间点正在运行的业务流程实例的状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-474">The orchestration engine saves the state of a running orchestration instance at various points.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-475">如果它需要 rehydrate 业务流程实例、 从受控关机，启动或从意外关闭恢复，它将从最后一个持久点运行业务流程实例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-475">If it needs to rehydrate the orchestration instance, start up from a controlled shutdown, or recover from an unexpected shutdown, it will run the orchestration instance from the last persistence point.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-476">才能持久地保存业务流程实例，所有对象直接或间接指您的业务流程的实例 （通过其他对象一样） 必须是可序列化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-476">In order to persist an orchestration instance, all object instances that your orchestration refers to directly or indirectly (as through other objects) must be serializable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-477">随着消息持久性频率 （需要持久保留数据的时间数） 将增加，总体性能下降。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-477">As message-persistence frequency (the number of times that data needs to be persisted) increases, overall performance decreases.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-478">实际上，每个持久性点是到数据库的往返行程，因此只要有可能减少通过避免或整合持久性点的持久性点的频率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-478">In effect, each persistence point is a round trip to the database, so whenever possible reduce the frequency of persistence points by avoiding or consolidating persistence points.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-479">请参阅下面有关持久性点发生时的详细信息的引用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-479">See the references below for more information regarding when persistence points occur.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-480">此分析检查以 10 个以上持久性点每秒平均。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-480">This analysis checks for more than 10 persistence points per second on average.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-481">这是一个常规的起始点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-481">This is a general starting point.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-482">引用：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-482">References:</span></span><br /><br /> <span |[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-485">: BizTalk 专用字节数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-485">:  BizTalk Private Bytes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-486">这是分配的专用内存的主机实例和类似于"\Process （*） \Private 字节数"性能计数器的兆字节。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-486">This is the megabytes of allocated private memory for the host instance and comparable to the “\Process(*)\Private Bytes” performance counter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-487">此分析将决定是否任何主机实例消耗的系统内存的大小，并在主机实例是否在内存消耗，随着时间的推移增加。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-487">This analysis determines whether any of the host instances are consuming a large size of the system's memory and whether the host instance is increasing in memory consumption over time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-488">有关详细信息的本主题中，请参阅 BizTalk 专用字节分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-488">Refer to BizTalk Private Bytes Analysis in this topic for more information.</span></span>|  
|[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-489">: BizTalk 假脱机表大小</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-489">:  BizTalk Spool Table Size</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-490">MessageBox 假脱机表包含在系统中的每个消息的记录 (活动或者正等着进行"垃圾回收")。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-490">The MessageBox spool table contains a record for each message in the system (active or waiting to be "garbage collected").</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-491">监视此表中的行数和系统负载增加可以轻松地查找最大可持续吞吐量时，每秒接收的消息数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-491">Monitoring the number of rows in this table and the number of messages received per second while increasing system load provides an easy way to find the maximum sustainable throughput.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-492">只需增加输入的负载，直至任一 1） 假脱机表开始无限增加或 2） 的每个第二个 plateaus、 准，并且该父级是最大可持续吞吐量接收的消息数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-492">Simply increase the input load until either 1) the spool table starts to grow indefinitely or 2) the number of messages received per second plateaus, whichever comes first, and that is your maximum sustainable throughput.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-493">总起来说，而不考虑其他指示符，此度量值将为你提供快速轻松地以评估是否或不在输出过度你的系统。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-493">In summary, regardless of other indicators, this measure will give you a quick and easy way to assess whether your system is being overdriven or not.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-494">如果 BizTalk 假脱机表大小为 on 上升趋势，然后限制由于失衡的消息传送速率 （输入的率超过输出率） 或者由于数据库大小限制可能会发生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-494">When the BizTalk spool tables size is on an increasing trend, then throttling due to imbalanced message delivery rate (input rate exceeds output rate) or throttling due to Database size may occur.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-495">此分析检查上升趋势 BizTalk 假脱机表大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-495">This analysis checks for an increasing trend in the BizTalk Spool Table Size.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-496">引用：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-496">References:</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-497">-了解 BizTalk Server 2004 SP1
