data-ttu-id="84b7a-499">-建议在测试时引擎在性能[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155294](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155294)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-499">-   Recommendations When Testing Engine Performance at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155294](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155294)</span></span>|  
|[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-500">： BizTalk 跟踪数据大小</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-500">:  BizTalk Tracking Data Size</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-501">BizTalk Server 处理越来越多的数据，你的系统上，BizTalk 跟踪数据库 (BizTalkDTADb) 就会继续增大。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-501">As BizTalk Server processes more and more data on your system, the BizTalk Tracking database (BizTalkDTADb) continues to grow in size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-502">不受控制的增长将会降低系统性能，并可能导致跟踪数据传送服务 (TDDS) 出错。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-502">Unchecked growth decreases system performance and may generate errors in the Tracking Data Delivery Service (TDDS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-503">除了一般的跟踪数据之外，跟踪的消息也会在 MessageBox 数据库中累积，导致磁盘性能下降。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-503">In addition to general tracking data, tracked messages can also accumulate in the MessageBox database, causing poor disk performance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-504">此分析检查上升趋势超过 5 MB 的每小时跟踪中的数据大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-504">This analysis checks for an increasing trend of more than 5 MB’s per hour in the tracking data size.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-505">参考：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-505">Reference:</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-506">存档和清除跟踪数据库在 BizTalk [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=153816](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=153816)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-506">Archiving and Purging the BizTalk Tracking Database at  [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=153816](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=153816)</span></span>|  
|[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-507">： BizTalk 中止的事务作用域</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-507">:  BizTalk Transactional Scopes Aborted</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-508">这是自主机实例启动后已中止的长时间运行或原子作用域数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-508">This is the number of long-running or atomic scopes that have been aborted since the host instance started.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-509">事务范围中止是发生在事务范围内业务流程失败。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-509">A transactional scope abort is a failure that occurs in a transaction scope within an orchestration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-510">请务必了解，都会调用作用域的补偿处理程序，仅当作用域已成功完成，但然后必须是撤消，因为确定周边范围 （由于更高版本中的过程可能会发生的故障） 而中止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-510">It is important to understand that the compensation handler of a scope is invoked only if the scope completed successfully, but then is required to be undone because a surrounding scope has decided to abort (due to failures that may occur later in the process).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-511">此外，如果事务中止发生的状态没有"自动"回滚。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-511">Also, no "auto" rollback of state occurs in case of a transaction abort.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-512">你可以实现这一目的以编程方式通过异常和补偿处理程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-512">You can achieve this outcome programmatically through the exception and compensation handlers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-513">事务范围中止不应该通常发生在生产环境中;因此，此分析将检查任何中止的事务作用域的匹配项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-513">Transactional scope aborts should not normally occur in a production environment; therefore, this analysis checks for the occurrence of any transactional scopes aborted.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-514">参考：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-514">Reference:</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-515">在 BizTalk Server 2004 跨事务[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108784](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108784)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-515">Transactions Across BizTalk Server 2004 at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108784](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108784)</span></span>|  
|[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-516">： 补偿 BizTalk 事务作用域</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-516">:  BizTalk Transactional Scopes Compensated</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-517">补偿可视为已成功提交到的某些错误条件的响应中的工作的逻辑撤消。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-517">Compensation can be thought of as a logical undo of the work that has been successfully committed in response to some error condition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-518">请务必了解，都会调用作用域的补偿处理程序，仅当作用域已成功完成，但然后必须是撤消，因为确定周边范围 （由于更高版本中的过程可能会发生的故障） 而中止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-518">It is important to understand that the compensation handler of a scope is invoked only if the scope completed successfully, but then is required to be undone because a surrounding scope has decided to abort (due to failures that may occur later in the process).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-519">此外，如果事务中止发生的状态没有"自动"回滚。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-519">Also, no "auto" rollback of state occurs in case of a transaction abort.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-520">这种回滚可以通过编写异常处理程序和补偿处理程序来实现。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-520">You can achieve this programmatically through the exception and compensation handlers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-521">事务范围补偿不应该通常发生在生产环境中;因此，此分析将检查任何中止的事务作用域的匹配项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-521">Transactional scope compensations should not normally occur in a production environment; therefore, this analysis checks for the occurrence of any transactional scopes aborted.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-522">参考： 事务跨在 BizTalk Server 2004 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108784](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108784)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-522">Reference: Transactions Across BizTalk Server 2004 at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108784](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=108784)</span></span>|  
|[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-523">: BizTalk 虚拟字节</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-523">:  BizTalk Virtual Bytes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-524">这是适用于主机实例的虚拟内存保留的兆字节。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-524">This is the megabytes reserved for virtual memory for the host instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-525">此分析将决定是否任何主机实例正在消耗大量的系统内存，且是否随时间推移的内存消耗中增加的主机实例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-525">This analysis determines whether any of the host instances are consuming a large amount of the system's memory and whether the host instance is increasing in memory consumption over time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-526">详细信息，请参阅本主题中的 BizTalk 虚拟字节分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-526">For more information, refer to BizTalk Virtual Bytes Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-527">: BizTalk 消息代理数据库会话限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-527">:  BizTalk Message Agent Database Session Throttling</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-528">这是到 MessageBox 相比限制设置其各自 BizTalk 打开数据库连接数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-528">This is the number of open database connections to the MessageBox compared to its respective BizTalk throttling setting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-529">"数据库连接每个 CPU"是最大并发数据库会话数 （每个 CPU) 限制开始之前允许。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-529">“Database connection per CPU” is the maximum number of concurrent database sessions (per CPU) allowed before throttling begins.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-530">详细信息，请参阅本主题中的为 BizTalk 消息代理数据库会话限制分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-530">For more information, refer to BizTalk Message Agent Database Session Throttling Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-531">: BizTalk 消息代理数据库会话限制阈值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-531">:  BizTalk Message Agent Database Session Throttling Threshold</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-532">这是到 MessageBox 的打开的数据库连接数的当前阈值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-532">This is the current threshold for the number of open database connections to the MessageBox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-533">"数据库连接每个 CPU"是最大并发数据库会话数 （每个 CPU) 限制开始之前允许。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-533">“Database connection per CPU” is the maximum number of concurrent database sessions (per CPU) allowed before throttling begins.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-534">详细信息，请参阅本主题中的为 BizTalk 消息代理数据库会话限制阈值分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-534">For more information, refer to BizTalk Message Agent Database Session Throttling Threshold Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-535">: BizTalk 消息代理进程内消息计数限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-535">:  BizTalk Message Agent In-process Message Count Throttling</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-536">这是处理服务类的并发消息数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-536">This is the number of concurrent messages that the service class is processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-537">在主机限制设置的"进程内消息每个 CPU"设置是最大的未处理的消息传递到的终结点管理器 (EPM) 或 XLANG 数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-537">The “In-process messages per CPU” setting in the Host Throttling Settings is the maximum number of messages delivered to the End Point Manager (EPM) or XLANG that have not been processed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-538">有关详细信息，请参阅本主题中的 BizTalk 消息代理进程内消息计数限制分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-538">For more information, refer to BizTalk Message Agent In-process Message Count Throttling Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|

|[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-543">: BizTalk 消息代理进程内存使用率 (MB) 限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-543">:  BizTalk Message Agent Process Memory Usage (MB) Throttling</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-544">这是当前进程 (MB) 的内存使用率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-544">This is the memory usage of current process (MB).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-545">BizTalk 进程内存限制可能要发布的批有陡峭的内存需求，或如果线程过多所处理的消息时发生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-545">BizTalk process memory throttling can occur if the batch to be published has steep memory requirements, or if too many threads are processing messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-546">有关详细信息，请参阅本主题中的 BizTalk 消息代理进程内存使用率 (MB) 限制分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-546">For more information, refer to BizTalk Message Agent Process Memory Usage (MB) Throttling Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-547">: BizTalk 消息代理进程内存使用率 (MB) 限制阈值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-547">:  BizTalk Message Agent Process Memory Usage (MB) Throttling Threshold</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-548">这是当前进程 (MB) 的内存使用量的当前阈值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-548">This is the current threshold for the memory usage of current process (MB).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-549">可能根据实际的此过程，并且其内存消耗模式的可用内存量动态调整阈值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-549">The threshold may be dynamically adjusted depending on the actual amount of memory available to this process and its memory consumption pattern.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-550">BizTalk 进程内存限制可能要发布的批有陡峭的内存需求，或如果线程过多所处理的消息时发生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-550">BizTalk process memory throttling can occur if the batch to be published has steep memory requirements, or if too many threads are processing messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-551">有关详细信息，请参阅 BizTalk 消息代理进程内存使用率 (MB) 限制阈值分析本主题中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-551">For more information, refer to BizTalk Message Agent Process memory usage (MB) Throttling Threshold Analysis in this topic.</span></span>|  
|[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-552">： 限制 BizTalk 消息代理线程计数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-552">:  BizTalk Message Agent Thread Count Throttling</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-553">BizTalk 进程中线程的总数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-553">The total number of threads in the BizTalk process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-554">"每个 CPU 线程数"是宿主进程包括由适配器使用的线程中的线程总数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-554">“Threads Per CPU” is the total number of threads in the host process including threads used by adapters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-555">如果超过此阈值，则 BizTalk Server 将尝试减小 EPM 线程池和消息代理线程池的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-555">If this threshold is exceeded, BizTalk Server will try to reduce the size of EPM thread pool and message agent thread pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-556">如果高负载可能导致创建大量线程，则在这种情况下，应启用基于线程的阻止功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-556">Thread based throttling should be enabled in scenarios where high load can lead to the creation of a large number of threads.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-557">此参数同时影响入站和出站阻止功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-557">This parameter affects both inbound and outbound throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-558">默认情况下，禁用基于线程限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-558">Thread based throttling is disabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-559">此分析将检查是否 BizTalk 线程计数大于 80%的限制阈值的值，该值指示可能的限制条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-559">This analysis checks whether the BizTalk Thread count is greater than 80 percent of the throttling threshold value indicating a throttling condition is likely.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-560">引用：</span><span Threads, DB sessions, and throttling at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106793](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106793)</span></span>|  
|[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServer2006r3](../includes/btsbiztalkserver2006r3-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-566">： 限制阈值 BizTalk 消息代理线程计数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-566">:  BizTalk Message Agent Thread Count Throttling Threshold</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-567">这是当前进程中的线程的总数的阈值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-567">This is the current threshold for the total number of threads in the process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-568">"每个 CPU 线程数"是宿主进程包括由适配器使用的线程中的线程总数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-568">“Threads Per CPU” is the total number of threads in the host process including threads used by adapters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-569">如果超过此阈值，则 BizTalk Server 将尝试减小 EPM 线程池和消息代理线程池的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-569">If this threshold is exceeded, BizTalk Server will try to reduce the size of EPM thread pool and message agent thread pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-570">在高负载可能导致大量的线程创建的情况下，应启用基于线程的限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-570">Thread-based throttling should be enabled in scenarios where high load can lead to the creation of a large number of threads.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-571">此参数同时影响入站和出站阻止功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-571">This parameter affects both inbound and outbound throttling.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-572">此分析检查是否将此限制设置设置为非默认值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-572">This analysis checks whether this throttling setting is set to a non-default value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-573">默认情况下，禁用基于线程限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-573">Thread based throttling is disabled by default.</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-574">引用：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-574">References:</span></span><br /><br /> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-575">-主机限制性能计数器在[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155285](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155285)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-575">-   Host Throttling Performance Counters at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155285](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155285)</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-576">-如何[!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)]实现主机限制在[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155286](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155286)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-576">-   How [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)] Implements Host Throttling at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155286](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155286)</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-577">-如何修改限制在设置的默认主机[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155296](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155296)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-577">-   How to Modify the Default Host Throttling Settings at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155296](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155296)</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-578">会影响适配器的性能的配置参数[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=154200](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=154200)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-578">-   Configuration Parameters that Affect Adapter Performance at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=154200](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=154200)</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-579">-线程，数据库会话和限制在[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106793](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106793)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-579">-   Threads, DB sessions, and throttling at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106793](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106793)</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="logicalphysical-disk-readwrite-latency-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-580">逻辑/物理磁盘读取/写入延迟分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-580">Logical/Physical Disk Read/Write Latency Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-581">Windows 检测磁盘性能瓶颈的最可靠方法是通过测量其响应时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-581">The most reliable way for Windows to detect a disk performance bottleneck is by measuring its response times.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-582">如果响应时间大于.025 （25 毫秒为单位），就是一个保守的阈值，然后可能发生明显减慢速度和影响用户的性能问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-582">If the response times are greater than .025 (25 milliseconds), which is a conservative threshold, then noticeable slow-downs and performance issues affecting users may be occurring.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-583">不佳的磁盘延迟的常见原因是磁盘碎片，性能缓存，在饱和 SAN，和太多的磁盘上的负载。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-583">Common causes of poor disk latency are disk fragmentation, performance cache, an over saturated SAN, and too much load on the disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-584">使用 SPA 工具来帮助确定前的文件和使用的磁盘的进程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-584">Use the SPA tool to help identify the top files and processes using the disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-585">也检查"过程 IO Data Operations/sec"和"过程 IO 其他 Operations/sec"以查看哪些进程消耗最多磁盘我 / O 的</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-585">Also check the “Process IO Data Operations/sec” and “Process IO Other Operations/sec” to see which processes are consuming the most disk I/O’s.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-586">请记住，性能监视器计数器不能指定涉及哪些文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-586">Keep in mind that performance monitor counters are unable to specify which files are involved.</span></span>  
  
### <a name="references"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-587">References</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-587">References</span></span>  
  
-   <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-588">允许在磁盘密集型问题[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=50669](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=50669)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-588">Ruling Out Disk-Bound Problems at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=50669](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=50669)</span></span>  
  
-   <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-589">如何识别使用在 Microsoft 服务器性能审查程序 (SPA) 工具进行磁盘性能瓶颈[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=98096](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=98096)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-589">How to Identify a Disk Performance Bottleneck Using the Microsoft Server Performance Advisor (SPA) Tool at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=98096](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=98096)</span></span>  
  
-   <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-590">在下载的 Microsoft 服务性能审查程序 (SPA) 的详细信息： [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=57769](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=57769)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-590">Download Details for Microsoft Service Performance Advisor (SPA) at: [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=57769](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=57769)</span></span>  
  
## <a name="logical-disk-transferssec"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-591">逻辑磁盘传输/次数/秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-591">Logical Disk Transfers/sec</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-592">"Disk Transfers/sec"是读取的速率和写入磁盘上的操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-592">“Disk Transfers/sec” is the rate of read and write operations on the disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-593">虽然磁盘传输并不是直接关联磁盘我 / O，它们请告知我们正在执行多少磁盘操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-593">While disk transfers are not a direct correlation to disk I/O's, they do tell us how many disk operations are occurring.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-594">如果你的平均顺序我 / O 的和随机我 / O，则你最终会得到约为 80 个我 / O 每秒作为常规的经验法则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-594">If you average out sequential I/O’s and random I/O's, then you end up with about 80 I/O's per second as a general rule of thumb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-595">因此，我们应该期望 SAN 驱动器来执行多个 80 我/O 每下的第二个时加载。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-595">Therefore, we should expect a SAN drive to perform more than 80 I/O's per second when under load.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-596">此分析检查以查看是否有任何逻辑磁盘的阈值展示较差的响应时间 （大于 25 秒 I/O 操作的响应时间）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-596">The thresholds for this analysis check to see whether any of the logical disks are showing poor response times (greater than 25 ms response times for I/O operations).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-597">如果是这样，我们应该知道每秒的时间来将达到或超过 80 个磁盘传输。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-597">If this is true, then we should expect the disk transfers per second to be at or above 80.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-598">如果没有，则磁盘体系结构需要进行调查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-598">If not, then the disk architecture needs to be investigated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-599">不佳的磁盘 I/O 的最常见原因是重载 SAN – 这意味着多个 LUN 正在使用小的物理磁盘阵列的位置的条件上的逻辑单元号 (LUN)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-599">The most common cause of poor disk I/O is logical unit number (LUN) overloading on the SAN – meaning the condition where more than one LUN is using the small physical disk array.</span></span>  
  
### <a name="reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-600">参考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-600">Reference</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-601">NT 服务器和磁盘子系统性能在[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106783](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106783)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-601">NT Server and Disk Subsystem Performance at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106783](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106783)</span></span>  
  
## <a name="available-memory-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-602">可用内存分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-602">Available Memory Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-603">"Available Mbytes"是可用兆字节为单位的计算机上运行的进程的物理内存量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-603">“Available Mbytes” is the amount of physical memory available to processes running on the computer, in megabytes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-604">虚拟内存管理器不断调整用在物理内存和磁盘上维护最小为操作系统和进程的可用字节数的空间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-604">The Virtual Memory Manager continually adjusts the space used in physical memory and on disk to maintain a minimum number of available bytes for the operating system and processes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-605">当可用字节数不多、 虚拟内存管理器会让进程工作集的增长或使它们通过删除每个新页面添加一个旧页稳定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-605">When available bytes are plentiful, the Virtual Memory Manager lets the working sets of processes grow, or keeps them stable by removing an old page for each new page added.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-606">几个可用字节时，虚拟内存管理器必须 trim 要维护的最低要求的进程的工作集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-606">When available bytes are few, the Virtual Memory Manager must trim the working sets of processes to maintain the minimum required.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-607">此分析将检查以确定总可用内存是否不足 – 10%可用处出现警告和在 5%可用的关键。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-607">This analysis checks to see whether the total available memory is low – Warning at 10 percent available and Critical at 5 percent available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-608">下降趋势的 10 MB 的每小时检测到，指示潜在的即将到来的内存不足情况时，警告也会得到通知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-608">A warning is also alerted when a decreasing trend of 10 MB’s per hour is detected, indicating a potential upcoming memory condition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-609">物理内存不足可能导致增加特权模式下 CPU 和系统延迟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-609">Low physical memory can cause increased privileged mode CPU and system delays.</span></span>  
  
### <a name="references"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-610">References</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-610">References</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-612">允许在内存密集型问题[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=62575](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=62575)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-612">Ruling Out Memory-Bound Problems at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=62575](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=62575)</span></span>  
  
## <a name="memory-leak-detection-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-613">内存泄漏检测分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-613">Memory Leak Detection Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-614">此分析将决定是否任何进程正在消耗大量的系统的内存，且是否在内存消耗，随着时间的推移增加过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-614">This analysis determines whether any of the processes are consuming a large amount of the system's memory and whether the process is increasing in memory consumption over time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-615">使用大量的内存的进程没什么关系，只要该过程将返回到系统内存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-615">A process consuming large portions of memory is okay as long as the process returns the memory back to the system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-616">查找增加图表的趋势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-616">Look for increasing trends in the chart.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-617">上升趋势长的一段时间内无法指示内存泄漏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-617">An increasing trend over a long period of time could indicate a memory leak.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-618">专用字节数是内存的当前大小 （字节），此进程已分配不能与其他进程共享。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-618">Private Bytes is the current size, in bytes, of memory that this process has allocated that cannot be shared with other processes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-619">此分析检查 10 MB 的每小时和 5 MB 的每小时增加趋势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-619">This analysis checks for 10 MB’s per hour and 5 MB’s per hour increasing trends.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-620">可用内存分析与相关联时使用此分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-620">Use this analysis in correlation with the Available Memory analysis.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-621">此外，请注意，新启动的进程将最初显示为内存泄漏时只需正常启动行为。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-621">Also, keep in mind that newly started processes will initially appear as a memory leak when it is simply normal startup behavior.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-622">进程继续占用内存并长的一段时间，不会释放内存时发生内存泄漏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-622">A memory leak occurs when a process continues to consume memory and does not release memory over a long period of time.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-623">如果您怀疑存在内存泄漏条件，然后安装并使用调试诊断工具。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-623">If you suspect a memory leak condition, then install and use the Debug Diag tool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-624">调试诊断工具的详细信息，请参阅引用部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-624">For more information on the Debug Diag Tool, see the references section.</span></span>  
  
### <a name="reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-625">参考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-625">Reference</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-626">调试在诊断工具 v1.1 [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106784](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106784)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-626">Debug Diagnostic Tool v1.1 at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106784](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106784)</span></span>  
  
## <a name="memory-pagessec-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-627">内存 Pages/sec 分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-627">Memory Pages/sec Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-628">此分析检查"页/秒"是否为高。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-628">This analysis checks to see whether the “Pages/sec” is high.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-629">如果高，然后系统可能内存不足尝试进行分页到磁盘的内存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-629">If it is high, then the system is likely running out of memory by trying to page the memory to the disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-630">"页/秒"是从读取或写入磁盘为解决强制分页错误页的速率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-630">“Pages/sec” is the rate at which pages are read from or written to disk to resolve hard page faults.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-631">此计数器是导致系统范围延迟的错误种类的主要指示器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-631">This counter is a primary indicator of the kinds of faults that cause system-wide delays.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-632">它是"Memory\Pages Input/sec"和"Memory\Pages Output/sec"的总和。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-632">It is the sum of “Memory\Pages Input/sec” and “Memory\Pages Output/sec”.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-633">则将计页数，因此它可以与其他页面，例如"Memory\Page Faults/sec"的计数进行比较。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-633">It is counted in numbers of pages, so it can be compared to other counts of pages, such as “Memory\Page Faults/sec”.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-634">此计数器始终应低于 1,000。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-634">This counter should always be below 1,000.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-635">此分析检查超过 1,000 个的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-635">This analysis checks for values above 1,000.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-636">可用内存分析和内存泄漏检测分析与相关联时使用此分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-636">Use this analysis in correlation with Available Memory Analysis and Memory Leak Detection analysis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-637">如果所有分析在同一时间都引发警报，这可能表示系统内存不足。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-637">If all analyses are throwing alerts at the same time, then this may indicate the system is running out of memory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-638">请按照本主题中的其他信息有关内存泄漏检测分析中所述的分析步骤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-638">Follow analysis steps mentioned in Additional Information Regarding Memory Leak Detection analysis in this topic.</span></span>  
  
### <a name="reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-639">参考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-639">Reference</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-640">允许在内存密集型问题[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=62575](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=62575)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-640">Ruling Out Memory-Bound Problems at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=62575](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=62575)</span></span>  
  
## <a name="memory-system-cache-resident-bytes-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-641">内存系统缓存驻留字节数分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-641">Memory System Cache Resident Bytes Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-642">"系统缓存驻留字节数"是的大小，以字节为单位，在文件系统缓存中的可分页操作系统代码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-642">“System Cache Resident Bytes” is the size, in bytes, of the pageable operating system code in the file system cache.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-643">此值只包括当前物理页面，并且不包括任何当前未驻留的虚拟内存页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-643">This value includes only current physical pages and does not include any virtual memory pages not currently resident.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-644">它就是显示在任务管理器中的系统缓存值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-644">It does equal the System Cache value shown in Task Manager.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-645">因此，此值可能小于的实际使用的文件系统缓存中的虚拟内存量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-645">As a result, this value may be smaller than the actual amount of virtual memory in use by the file system cache.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-646">此值是一个组件的"内存\\\System 代码驻留字节数"，它表示所有当前正在物理内存的可分页操作系统代码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-646">This value is a component of “Memory\\\System Code Resident Bytes”, which represents all pageable operating system code that is currently in physical memory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-647">此计数器显示上次观测的值仅;它不是平均值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-647">This counter displays the last observed value only; it is not an average.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-648">此分析检查上升趋势的 10 MB 的每小时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-648">This analysis checks for an increasing trend of 10 MB’s per hour.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-649">承受负载时，服务器可能使用的系统缓存，以便缓存如磁盘 I/O 活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-649">Under load, a server might use the system cache in order to cache I/O activity such as disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-650">将相关联时使用与过程 IO Data Operations/sec 和进程 IO 其他操作数/秒分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-650">Use in correlation with Process IO Data Operations/sec and Process IO Other Operations/sec analyses.</span></span>  
  
## <a name="processor-utilization-analysis-and-excessive-processor-use-by-processes"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-651">处理器利用率分析和进程过多的处理器使用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-651">Processor Utilization Analysis and Excessive Processor Use by Processes</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-652">"%Processor Time"是处理器执行非闲置线程所花的运行时间的百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-652">“% Processor Time” is the percentage of elapsed time that the processor spends to execute a non-idle thread.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-653">它是通过测量采样间隔期间，空闲线程处于活动状态的持续时间然后时间然后减去间隔持续时间计算的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-653">It is calculated by measuring the duration the idle thread is active in the sample interval, and then subtracting that time from the interval duration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-654">（每个处理器有占用时钟周期当没有其他线程准备好运行的空闲线程）。此计数器是处理器活动的主要指示器，并显示在采样间隔期间观察到的忙碌时间的平均百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-654">(Each processor has an idle thread that consumes cycles when no other threads are ready to run.) This counter is the primary indicator of processor activity and displays the average percentage of busy time observed during the sample interval.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-655">它被通过监视服务处于非活动状态的时间，然后从 100%减去该值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-655">It is calculated by monitoring the time that the service is inactive, and subtracting that value from 100 percent.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-656">此分析检查大于每个单个处理器上的 60%的利用率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-656">This analysis checks for utilization greater than 60 percent on each individual processor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-657">如果是这样，确定它是否是高用户模式 CPU 或高特权模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-657">If so, determine whether it is high user mode CPU or high privileged mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-658">如果高特权模式下 CPU 怀疑有问题，请参阅"特权模式 CPU 分析"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-658">If high privileged mode CPU is suspected, then see the “Privileged Mode CPU Analysis”.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-659">如果怀疑用户模式下处理器瓶颈，则可以考虑使用进程探查器分析导致高 CPU 使用的函数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-659">If a user-mode processor bottleneck is suspected, then consider using a process profiler to analyze the functions causing the high CPU consumption.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-660">请参阅"如何为： 标识导致高用户模式 CPU 瓶颈的出现针对服务器应用程序在生产环境中的函数"的详细信息的参考部分中的文章。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-660">See “How To: Identify Functions causing a High User-mode CPU Bottleneck for Server Applications in a Production Environment” article in the references section for more information.</span></span>  
  
## <a name="processor-queue-length-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-661">处理器队列长度分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-661">Processor Queue Length Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-662">"处理器队列长度"是处理器队列中的线程数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-662">“Processor Queue Length” is the number of threads in the processor queue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-663">与磁盘计数器，此计数器只显示就绪线程，不正在运行的线程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-663">Unlike the disk counters, this counter shows ready threads only, not threads that are running.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-664">没有单个队列的处理器时间百分比甚至具有多个处理器的计算机上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-664">There is a single queue for processor time even on computers with multiple processors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-665">因此，如果计算机具有多个处理器，需要此值除以处理工作负载的处理器数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-665">Therefore, if a computer has multiple processors, you need to divide this value by the number of processors servicing the workload.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-666">每个处理器少于 10 个线程的持续的处理器队列是通常可接受，取决于工作负荷。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-666">A sustained processor queue of less than 10 threads per processor is normally acceptable, dependent of the workload.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-667">此分析将决定是否平均处理器队列长度超过处理器的数目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-667">This analysis determines whether the average processor queue length exceeds the number of processors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-668">如果是这样，则这可能表示处理器瓶颈。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-668">If so, then this could indicate a processor bottleneck.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-669">与特权模式 CPU 分析和由进程过多的处理器使用相关联时使用此分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-669">Use this analysis in correlation with Privileged Mode CPU Analysis and Excessive Processor Use by Process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-670">处理器队列为是准备好，但不是能够执行的处理器，因为当前正在执行另一个活动线程的线程的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-670">The processor queue is the collection of threads that are ready but not able to be executed by the processor because another active thread is currently executing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-671">持续或重复的更多的处理器数目是处理器瓶颈更好地指示线程的队列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-671">A sustained or recurring queue of more threads than number of processors is a good indication of a processor bottleneck.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-672">你可以结合使用此计数器"处理器\\%Processor Time"计数器以确定你的应用程序是否可以受益于更多的 Cpu。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-672">You can use this counter in conjunction with the “Processor\\% Processor Time” counter to determine whether your application can benefit from more CPUs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-673">没有单个队列的处理器时间，即使是在多处理器计算机上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-673">There is a single queue for processor time, even on multiprocessor computers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-674">因此，在多处理器计算机中，将"处理器队列长度"(PQL) 值除以处理工作负载的处理器数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-674">Therefore, in a multiprocessor computer, divide the “Processor Queue Length” (PQL) value by the number of processors servicing the workload</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-675">如果 CPU 非常繁忙 （90%和更高的利用率） 和 PQL 平均值高于一致的处理器数，则可能存在处理器瓶颈，无法受益于更多的 Cpu。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-675">If the CPU is very busy (90 percent and higher utilization) and the PQL average is consistently higher than the number of processors, then you may have a processor bottleneck that could benefit from additional CPUs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-676">或者，你可能会减少的线程和应用程序级别的队列数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-676">Or, you could reduce the number of threads and queue at the application level.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-677">这将导致减少上下文切换，这很好的降低 CPU 负载。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-677">This will cause less context switching, which is good for reducing CPU load.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-678">低 CPU 使用率高 PQL 的常见原因是时间的处理器时间的请求到达随机，和线程要求异常长从处理器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-678">The common reason for a high PQL with low CPU utilization is that requests for processor time arrive randomly, and threads demand irregular amounts of time from the processor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-679">这意味着处理器不成为瓶颈。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-679">This means that the processor is not a bottleneck.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-680">相反，工作线程处理逻辑，需要能够改进。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-680">Instead, your threading logic that needs to be improved.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-681">如果怀疑用户模式下处理器瓶颈，则可以考虑使用进程探查器分析导致高 CPU 使用的函数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-681">If a user-mode processor bottleneck is suspected, then consider using a process profiler to analyze the functions causing the high CPU consumption.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-682">请参阅"如何为： 标识导致高用户模式 CPU 瓶颈的出现针对服务器应用程序在生产环境中的函数"的详细信息的参考部分中的文章。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-682">See the “How To: Identify Functions causing a High User-mode CPU Bottleneck for Server Applications in a Production Environment” article in the references section for more information.</span></span>  
  
## <a name="privileged-mode-cpu-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-683">特权模式下 CPU 分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-683">Privileged Mode CPU Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-684">此计数器指示在特权模式下运行的线程的时间的百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-684">This counter indicates the percentage of time a thread runs in privileged mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-685">当你的应用程序调用时 （例如，可执行文件或网络 I/O 或分配内存） 的操作系统功能时，这些操作系统功能在特权模式下执行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-685">When your application calls operating system functions (for example to perform file or network I/O or to allocate memory), these operating system functions are executed in privileged mode.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-686">高特权模式下 CPU 指示计算机花费在与实际 （用户模式） 的系统 I/O 工作中太多时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-686">High privileged mode CPU indicates that the computer is spending too much time in system I/O versus real (user mode) work.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-687">"%Privileged Time"是进程线程在特权模式下执行代码所用的运行时间的百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-687">“% Privileged Time” is the percentage of elapsed time that the process threads spent executing code in privileged mode.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-688">当调用 Windows 系统服务时，服务将通常运行在特权模式下，若要获取对系统专有数据的访问权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-688">When a Windows system service is called, the service will often run in privileged mode to gain access to system-private data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-689">此类数据不会发生访问由在用户模式下执行的线程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-689">Such data is protected from access by threads executing in user mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-690">对系统的调用可以显式或隐式的如页错误或中断。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-690">Calls to the system can be explicit or implicit, such as page faults or interrupts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-691">不像某些早期的操作系统，Windows 使用进程边界对于除了传统的保护的用户和特权的模式的子系统保护。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-691">Unlike some early operating systems, Windows uses process boundaries for subsystem protection in addition to the traditional protection of user and privileged modes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-692">代表应用程序通过 Windows 某些工作可能会出现在过程中的特权时间除了其他子系统进程中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-692">Some work done by Windows on behalf of the application might appear in other subsystem processes in addition to the privileged time in the process.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-693">此分析将检查以查看特权模式下 CPU 是否占用了超过 30%的总 CPU。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-693">This analysis checks to see whether privileged mode CPU is consuming more than 30 percent of total CPU.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-694">如果这样，则可能的 CPU 消耗是才导致的网络、 内存或磁盘 I/O 等处理器以外的另一个瓶颈。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-694">If so, then the CPU consumption is likely caused by another bottleneck other than the processor such as network, memory, or disk I/O.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-695">使用相关联时使用 %Interrupt Time 和高上下文切换分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-695">Use in correlation with % Interrupt Time and High Context Switching analyses.</span></span>  
  
## <a name="high-context-switching-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-696">高上下文切换分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-696">High Context Switching Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-697">较高优先级的线程会抢占较低的优先级线程当前正在运行或高优先级的线程块时，会发生情况的上下文切换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-697">A context switch happens when a higher priority thread preempts a lower priority thread that is currently running or when a high priority thread blocks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-698">当多个线程共享相同的优先级级别，则会发生的上下文切换的高级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-698">High levels of context switching can occur when many threads share the same priority level.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-699">这通常指示线程过多在争夺系统上的处理器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-699">This often indicates that too many threads are competing for the processors on the system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-700">如果你看不到更处理器利用率，请参阅非常低级别的上下文切换，则可能表示线程被阻止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-700">If you do not see much processor utilization and you see very low levels of context switching, it could indicate that threads are blocked.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-701">高特权模式下，CPU 和总体 CPU 时应仅调查高上下文切换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-701">High context switching should only be investigated when privileged mode CPU and overall CPU is high.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-702">一般情况下，上下文切换速率小于每个处理器每秒 5,000 的不是值得担心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-702">As a general rule, context switching rates of less than 5,000 per second per processor are not worth worrying about.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-703">如果上下文切换率超过每个处理器每秒的 15000，则一个约束。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-703">If context switching rates exceed 15,000 per second per processor, then there is a constraint.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-704">此分析检查高 CPU、 高特权模式下 CPU 和高 （大于为每个处理器的 5,000） 系统上下文切换每秒在同一时间发生的所有。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-704">This analysis checks for high CPU, high privileged mode CPU, and high (greater than 5,000 per processor) system context switches per second all occurring at the same time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-705">如果出现高上下文切换，然后减少线程和系统上运行的进程的数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-705">If high context switching is occurring, then reduce the number of threads and processes running on the system.</span></span>  
  
## <a name="biztalk-high-database-sessions-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-706">BizTalk 高数据库会话分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-706">BizTalk High Database Sessions Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-707">此计数器有两个可能的值即正常 (0)，或超出了 (1)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-707">This counter has two possible values namely normal (0) or exceeded (1).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-708">此分析检查的值为 1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-708">This analysis checks for a value of 1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-709">如果是这样，BizTalk 超过了允许的数据库会话数的阈值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-709">If so, BizTalk has exceeded the threshold of the number of database sessions permitted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-710">此值由 BizTalk 主机限制设置中的"每个 CPU 的数据库连接"值控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-710">This value is controlled by the “Database connection per CPU” value in the BizTalk Host Throttling settings.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-711">"数据库连接每个 CPU"是最大并发数据库会话数 （每个 CPU) 限制开始之前允许。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-711">“Database connection per CPU” is the maximum number of concurrent database sessions (per CPU) allowed before throttling begins.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-712">此计数不包括通用的每主机会话池中的空闲数据库会话数，并且只对主机实例实际使用的会话数进行此检查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-712">The idle database sessions in the common per-host session pool do not add to this count, and this check is made strictly on the number of sessions actually being used by the host instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-713">默认情况下; 禁用此选项通常情况下，此设置应仅启用如果数据库服务器是瓶颈或低端的数据库服务器在 BizTalk Server 系统中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-713">This option is disabled by default; typically, this setting should only be enabled if the database server is a bottleneck or for low-end database servers in the BizTalk Server system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-714">可以通过使用 BizTalk:Message 代理性能对象类别下的数据库会话性能计数器来监视活动数据库连接数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-714">You can monitor the number of active database connections by using the database session performance counter under the BizTalk:Message Agent performance object category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-715">此参数只影响出站消息阻止功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-715">This parameter only affects outbound message throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-716">输入值 0 可以禁用基于数据库会话数的阻止功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-716">Enter a value of 0 to disable throttling that is based on the number of database sessions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-717">默认值为 0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-717">The default value is 0.</span></span>  
  
> [!NOTE]  
>  <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-718">"MaxWorkerThreads"注册表项会影响到 BizTalk 可用线程的数目，并且有助于如果 BizTalk 线程中的大部分均忙于数据库连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-718">The “MaxWorkerThreads” registry key influences the number threads available to BizTalk and may help if most of the BizTalk threads are busy with database connections.</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-high-database-size-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-724">BizTalk 高数据库大小分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-724">BizTalk High Database Size Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-725">此计数器是指此进程已发布的数据库队列中的消息数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-725">This counter refers to the number of messages in the database queues that this process has published.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-726">此值按所有主机队列表中的项数以及后台处理表和跟踪表中的项数来衡量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-726">This value is measured by the number of items in the queue tables for all hosts and the number of items in the spool and tracking tables.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-727">队列包括工作队列、 状态队列和挂起的队列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-727">Queue includes the work queue, the state queue and the suspended queue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-728">如果要将某一进程发布到多个队列，则此计数器将反映所有队列的加权平均值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-728">If a process is publishing to multiple queues, this counter reflects the weighted average of all the queues.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-729">如果重新启动该主机，则内存中保留的统计信息将丢失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-729">If the host is restarted, statistics held in memory are lost.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-730">由于涉及一些开销，请将恢复 BizTalk Server，仅当有至少 100 发布，5%的总发布重新启动的主机进程内收集统计信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-730">Since some overhead is involved, BizTalk Server will resume gathering statistics only when there are at least 100 publishes, with 5 percent of the total publishes within the restarted host process.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-731">为数据库阈值中的消息计数列出的条件之一时，此计数器将设置为值为 1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-731">This counter will be set to a value of 1 if either of the conditions listed for the message count in database threshold occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-732">此阈值记录在该主题如何修改默认主机限制设置下面引用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-732">This threshold is documented in the topic How to Modify the Default Host Throttling Settings referenced below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-733">默认情况下，主机消息限制阈值的数据库中的计数设置为值为 50000，就会触发在下列情况下的限制条件：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-733">By default the host message count in database throttling threshold is set to a value of 50,000, which will trigger a throttling condition under the following circumstances:</span></span>  
  
-   <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-734">主机实例发布到订阅主机的工作、状态和已挂起队列的消息总数超过 50,000。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-734">The total number of messages published by the host instance to the work, state, and suspended queues of the subscribing hosts exceeds 50,000.</span></span>  
  
-   <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-735">后台处理表或跟踪表中的消息数超过 500,000。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-735">The number of messages in the spool table or the tracking table exceeds 500,000 messages.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-736">在计算中使用数据库邮件计数中包括挂起的消息，因为限制的消息发布即使 BizTalk server 遇到低或没有负载会发生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-736">Since suspended messages are included in the message count in database calculation, throttling of message publishing can occur even if the BizTalk server is experiencing low or no load.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-737">此分析检查的值为 1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-737">This analysis checks for a value of 1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-738">如果发生这种情况，请考虑将减少在数据库中的消息数的操作过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-738">If this occurs, then consider a course of action that will reduce the number of messages in the database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-739">例如，确保 BizTalk SQL Server 作业运行正常并使用 BizTalk 管理控制台中的组中心数据库来确定是否将消息生成向上引起的大量的挂起的消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-739">For example, ensure the BizTalk SQL Server jobs are running without error and use the Group Hub in the BizTalk Administration console to determine whether message build up is caused by large numbers of suspended messages.</span></span>  
  
### <a name="references"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-740">References</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-740">References</span></span>  
  
-   <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-741">挂起的消息都包含在数据库限制阈值中的消息计数[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155304](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155304)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-741">Suspended Messages are Included in the Message Count in Database Throttling Threshold at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155304](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155304)</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-high-in-process-message-count-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-744">BizTalk 高进程内消息计数分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-744">BizTalk High In-Process Message Count Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-745">在主机限制设置的"进程内消息每个 CPU"设置是最大的未处理的消息传递到的终结点管理器 (EPM) 或 XLANG 数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-745">The “In-process messages per CPU” setting in the Host Throttling Settings is the maximum number of messages delivered to the End Point Manager (EPM) or XLANG that have not been processed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-746">此数字不包括从但仍等待中内存中队列的传递的数据库中检索的消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-746">This number does not include the messages retrieved from database but still waiting for delivery in the in-memory queue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-747">可以通过使用 BizTalk:Message 代理性能对象类别下的进程内消息计数性能计数器来监视进程内消息数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-747">You can monitor the number of in-Process Messages by using the In-process message count performance counter under the BizTalk:Message Agent performance object category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-748">在考虑限制条件时，此参数提供的限制机制提示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-748">This parameter provides a hint to the throttling mechanism when considering throttling conditions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-749">实际阈值可能会自我优化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-749">The actual threshold is subject to self-tuning.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-750">你可以通过监视的进程内消息计数性能计数器来验证实际阈值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-750">You can verify the actual threshold by monitoring the in-process message count performance counter.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-751">此参数可以设置为较小的值对于大型消息方案，其中的平均消息大小较高，或消息的处理可能需要大量的消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-751">This parameter can be set to a smaller value for large message scenarios, where either the average message size is high, or the processing of messages may require a large number of messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-752">这将是很明显，如果一个方案遇到过于频繁基于内存的限制和内存阈值获取自动调整为大体上低的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-752">This would be evident if a scenario experiences memory-based throttling too often and if the memory threshold gets auto-adjusted to a substantially low value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-753">这样将指示出站传输应降低同时处理的消息数以避免占用过高内存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-753">Such behavior would indicate that the outbound transport should process fewer messages concurrently to avoid excessive memory usage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-754">此外，如果适配器一次处理多个消息（例如在向限制并行连接数的服务器发送消息时）可获得更高效率，则可以将此参数优化为低于默认值的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-754">Also, for scenarios where the adapter is more efficient when processing a few messages at a time (for example, when sending to a server that limits concurrent connections), this parameter may be tuned to a lower value than the default.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-755">此分析检查的进程内消息计数高计数器以确定是否发生这种类型的限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-755">This analysis checks the High In-Process Message Count counter to determine whether this kind of throttling is occurring.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-756">如果是这样，请考虑调整"每 CPU 邮件进程内"设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-756">If so, consider adjusting the “In-Process messages per CPU” setting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-757">此参数只影响出站消息阻止功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-757">This parameter only affects outbound message throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-758">在禁用限制基于每个 CPU 进程内消息数"进程内消息每个 CPU"设置中输入的值为 0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-758">Enter a value of 0 in the “In-Process messages per CPU” setting to disable throttling based on the number of in-process messages per CPU.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-759">"进程内消息每个 CPU"设置的默认值为 1000。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-759">The default value for the “In-Process messages per CPU” setting is 1,000.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-760">请注意，修改此值还可以影响在低延迟的消息和/或 BizTalk 资源的效率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-760">Note that modifying this value can also have an impact on low latency of messages and/or the efficiency of BizTalk resources.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-763">限制在性能计数器的主机[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155285](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155285)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-763">Host Throttling Performance Counters at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155285](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155285)</span></span>  
  
## <a name="biztalk-high-message-delivery-rate-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-764">BizTalk 高邮件传递速率分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-764">BizTalk High Message Delivery Rate Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-765">对于出站 （发送） 的消息，BizTalk Server 限制的消息传送，如果主机实例的消息传递传入速率超过传出速率消息传递 * 指定的速率 overdrive 因子 （%） 的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-765">For outbound (delivered) messages, BizTalk Server throttles delivery of messages if the message delivery incoming rate for the host instance exceeds the message delivery outgoing rate * the specified rate overdrive factor (percent) value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-766">在消息处理限制设置对话框上，速率 overdrive 因素 （百分比） 参数是可配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-766">The rate overdrive factor (percent) parameter is configurable on the Message Processing Throttling Settings dialog box.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-767">基于速率限制的出站消息是主要通过将从内存中队列中删除消息，并将消息传递到的终结点管理器 (EPM) 或业务流程引擎会为处理前的延迟实现的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-767">Rate-based throttling for outbound messages is accomplished primarily by inducing a delay before removing the messages from the in-memory queue and delivering the messages to the End Point Manager (EPM) or orchestration engine for processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-768">不执行任何其他操作来完成基于速率限制的出站消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-768">No other action is taken to accomplish rate-based throttling for outbound messages.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-769">出站阻止可能导致消息送达延迟，消息可能会在内存中队列中堆积，并可能导致出列线程被阻止，直到阻止条件得以缓解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-769">Outbound throttling can cause delayed message delivery and messages may build up in the in-memory queue and cause de-queue threads to be blocked until the throttling condition is mitigated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-770">当取消排队线程被阻止，从消息框中放入内存中队列进行出站传递提取任何额外的消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-770">When de-queue threads are blocked, no additional messages are pulled from the MessageBox into the in-memory queue for outbound delivery.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-771">此分析检查的值为 1 中的高的消息传送速率计数器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-771">This analysis checks for a value of 1 in the High Message Delivery Rate counter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-772">高的消息传送速率可能引起高处理复杂性、 慢速的出站适配器或暂时的系统资源不足。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-772">High message delivery rates can be caused by high processing complexity, slow outbound adapters, or a momentary shortage of system resources.</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-high-process-memory-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-777">BizTalk 高进程内存分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-777">BizTalk High Process Memory Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-778">限制阈值设置的 BizTalk 进程内存使用量是内存的相比工作集大小和进程的总可用虚拟内存的总和，如果输入从 1 到 100 之间的值所使用百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-778">The BizTalk Process Memory usage throttling threshold setting is the percentage of memory used compared to the sum of the working set size and total available virtual memory for the process if a value from 1 through 100 is entered.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-779">默认情况下，BizTalk 进程内存使用情况限制设置为 25。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-779">By default, the BizTalk Process Memory Usage throttling setting is 25.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-780">在指定百分比值时，将按固定的时间间隔来重新计算进程内存阈值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-780">When a percentage value is specified the process memory threshold is recalculated at regular intervals.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-781">如果用户指定一个百分比值，它是根据计算为提交和当前的进程内存使用量的可用内存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-781">If the user specifies a percentage value, it is computed based on the available memory to commit and the current Process Memory usage.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-782">此分析检查 1 中的高进程内存计数器的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-782">This analysis checks for a value of 1 in the High Process Memory counter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-783">如果发生这种情况，然后尝试通过使用调试诊断确定内存增加的原因 （请参阅在内存泄漏检测分析中的引用）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-783">If this occurs, then try to determine the cause of the memory increase by using Debug Diag (see references in Memory Leak Detection analysis).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-784">请注意，是正常的进程在启动和这期间使用的内存很大一部分它可能最初显示为内存泄漏，但进程无法释放它不再需要从而减少的可用我的内存，则会发生了真正的内存泄漏随着时间的推移 mory。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-784">Note that is it normal for processes to consume a large portion of memory during startup and this may initially appear as a memory leak, but a true memory leak occurs when a process fails to release memory that it no longer needs, thereby reducing the amount of available memory over time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-785">有关如何以一般方式分析 BizTalk 中的进程内存泄漏，请参阅下面的"如何为捕获内存转储的进程，是泄露内存"引用和/或"内存泄漏检测"分析 PAL 中的有关详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-785">See the “How to Capture a Memory Dump of a Process that is Leaking Memory” reference below and/or the “Memory Leak Detection” analysis in PAL for more information on how to generically analyze process memory leaks in BizTalk.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-786">如果要发布的批具有陡峭的内存要求高的进程内存限制可能发生或线程过多所处理的消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-786">High process memory throttling can occur if the batch to be published has steep memory requirements, or too many threads are processing messages.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-787">如果系统看起来过度限制，请考虑增加主机进程内存使用情况阈值与关联的值，并验证主机实例不会生成"内存不足"错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-787">If the system appears to be over-throttling, consider increasing the value associated with the process memory usage threshold for the host and verify that the host instance does not generate an "out of memory" error.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-788">如果通过增加进程内存使用情况阈值引发"内存不足"错误，请考虑减少内部消息队列大小的值，并且进程内每个 CPU 阈值的消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-788">If an "out of memory" error is raised by increasing the process memory usage threshold, then consider reducing the values for the internal message queue size and In-process messages per CPU thresholds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-789">此策略特别适用于大型消息处理方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-789">This strategy is particularly relevant in large message processing scenarios.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-790">此外，此值应设置为具有较大内存要求每个消息的方案的低值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-790">In addition, this value should be set to a low value for scenarios having large memory requirement per message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-791">设置较低的值将在早期限制开始运作，并使进程内的内存分解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-791">Setting a low value will kick in throttling early on and prevent a memory explosion within the process.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-792">如果你的 BizTalk server 定期运行虚拟内存不足时，请考虑 BizTalk Server 64 位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-792">If your BizTalk server regularly runs out of virtual memory, then consider BizTalk Server 64-bit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-793">在 64 位服务器上的每个进程可以解决最高支持 4 TB 的虚拟内存与在 32 位 2 GB。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-793">Each process on 64-bit servers can address up to 4 TB’s of virtual memory versus the 2 GB’s in 32-bit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-794">一般情况下，强烈建议 BizTalk 64 位和 64 位 SQL Server。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-794">In general, 64-bit BizTalk and 64-bit SQL Server is highly recommended.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-795">请参阅有关详细信息"BizTalk Server 64 位支持"参考。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-795">See the “BizTalk Server 64-bit Support” reference for more information.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-798">如何修改限制在设置的默认主机[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155296](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155296)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-798">How to Modify the Default Host Throttling Settings at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155296](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=155296)</span></span>  
  
-   <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-799">如何捕获在泄漏内存的进程内存转储[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155305](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155305)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-799">How to Capture a Memory Dump of a Process that is Leaking Memory at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155305](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155305)</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-high-system-memory-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-801">BizTalk 高系统内存分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-801">BizTalk High System Memory Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-802">BizTalk 物理内存使用情况限制阈值设置为输入相比从 1 到 100 之间的可用物理内存的值如果总量的内存消耗的百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-802">The BizTalk Physical Memory usage throttling threshold setting is the percentage of memory consumption compared to the total amount of available physical memory if a value from 1 through 100 is entered.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-803">如果输入大于 100 的值，此设置也可以在兆字节为单位的可用物理内存的总量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-803">This setting can also be the total amount of available physical memory in megabytes if a value greater than 100 is entered.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-804">输入值 0 可以禁用基于物理内存使用率的阻止功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-804">Enter a value of 0 to disable throttling based on physical memory usage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-805">默认值为 0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-805">The default value is 0.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-806">此分析检查 1 中的较高的系统内存计数器的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-806">This analysis checks for a value of 1 in the High System Memory counter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-807">由于这样将度量系统内存总量，因此如果非 BizTalk Server 进程占用过多的系统内存，则可能会触发阻止条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-807">Since this measures total system memory, a throttling condition may be triggered if non-BizTalk Server processes are consuming an extensive amount of system memory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-808">因此如果发生这种情况，最好的方法是确定哪些进程使用在大多数物理内存和/或向服务器添加额外的物理内存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-808">Therefore if this occurs, the best approach is to identify which processes are consuming the most physical memory and/or add additional physical memory to the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-809">此外，请考虑减少 EPM 线程池的默认大小和/或适配器批的大小，从而减少负载。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-809">Also, consider reducing load by reducing the default size of the EPM thread pool, and/or the size of adapter batches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-810">有关详细信息，请参阅 PAL 中的内存泄漏检测分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-810">For more information, see the Memory Leak Detection analysis in PAL.</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-high-thread-count-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-815">BizTalk 高线程计数分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-815">BizTalk High Thread Count Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-816">"每个 CPU 线程数"是宿主进程包括由适配器使用的线程中的线程总数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-816">“Threads Per CPU” is the total number of threads in the host process including threads used by adapters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-817">如果超出此阈值，BizTalk Server 将尝试减小 EPM 线程池和消息代理线程池的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-817">If this threshold is exceeded, BizTalk Server will try to reduce the size of the EPM thread pool and message agent thread pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-818">如果高负载可能导致创建大量线程，则在这种情况下，应启用基于线程的阻止功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-818">Thread based throttling should be enabled in scenarios where high load can lead to the creation of a large number of threads.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-819">此参数同时影响入站和出站阻止功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-819">This parameter affects both inbound and outbound throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-820">默认情况下，禁用基于线程限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-820">Thread based throttling is disabled by default.</span></span>  
  
> [!NOTE]  
>  <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-821">用户指定的值用作一项准则，并且主机动态自行调整此阈值基于内存使用模式和线程要求的过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-821">The user-specified value is used as a guideline, and the host may dynamically self-tune this threshold value based on the memory usage patterns and thread requirements of the process.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-822">此分析检查值为高线程计数计数器中的 1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-822">This analysis checks for a value of 1 in the High Thread Count counter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-823">考虑调整不同线程池的大小，以确保系统不会创建大量线程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-823">Consider adjusting the different thread pool sizes to ensure that the system does not create a large number of threads.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-824">每第二个分析，以确定是否操作系统已经饱和与线程过多，但在大多数情况下，高线程计数原因比的后端数据库上的 BizTalk server 的详细争用，可以使用上下文切换关联此分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-824">This analysis can be correlated with Context Switches per Second analysis to determine whether the operating system is saturated with too many threads, but in most cases high thread counts cause more contention on the backend database than on the BizTalk server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-825">有关修改线程池大小的详细信息请参阅如何修改默认主机限制中的设置的引用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-825">For more information about modifying the thread pool sizes see How to Modify the Default Host Throttling Settings in references.</span></span>
