 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-832">BizTalk 入站延迟 AnalysisAverage 延迟消息引擎文档从接收适配器之前发布到消息框的时间 （毫秒）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-832">BizTalk Inbound Latency AnalysisAverage latency in milliseconds from when the messaging engine receives a document from the adapter until the time it is published to the message box.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-833">减少延迟是重要的 BizTalk，某些用户因此跟踪时间文档在入站适配器中的花费多少是很重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-833">Reducing latency is important to some users of BizTalk, therefore tracking how much time documents spend in the inbound adapter is important.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-834">下面是一个图，显示延迟的衡量标准。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-834">Here is a chart showing how latency is measured.</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-835">1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-835">1</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-836">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-836">2</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-837">3</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-837">3</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-838">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-838">4</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-839">5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-839">5</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-840">6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-840">6</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-841">适配器接收消息，并提交在这些性能计数器中捕获它与引擎之前消息提供不引擎适配器中完成的工作</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-841">Adapter receives message and submits it to the engine, work done in adapter before message is given to engine not captured in these perf counters</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-842">引擎从适配器接收消息，执行接收管道、 映射、 订阅计算，保留在数据库中的消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-842">Engine receives message from adapter, executes receive pipeline, map, subscription evaluation, persist message in DB.</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-843">业务流程或请求-响应端口将运行并生成响应消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-843">Orchestration or Solicit-Response port runs and generates a response message.</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-844">响应消息取消排队消息引擎中，执行发送管道，映射。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-844">Response message is dequeued in messaging engine, execute the send pipeline, map.</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-845">消息传递引擎赋予适配器的响应消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-845">Messaging engine gives response message to adapter.</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-846">适配器通知引擎消息就可全部完成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-846">Adapter informs engine message is all done.</span></span>|  
||<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-847">I</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-847">I</span></span>|||||  
||<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-848">RR</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-848">RR</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-849">RR</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-849">RR</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-850">RR</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-850">RR</span></span>|||  
||||<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-851">O</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-851">O</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-852">O</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-852">O</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-853">O</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-853">O</span></span>|  
|||||<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-854">OA</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-854">OA</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-855">OA</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-855">OA</span></span>|  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-856">我 = 入站的延迟</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-856">I = Inbound Latency</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-857">RR = 请求的响应延迟时间</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-857">RR = Request Response Latency</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-858">O = 出站延迟</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-858">O = Outbound Latency</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-859">OA = 出站适配器延迟</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-859">OA = Outbound Adapter Latency</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-860">假设低延迟环境，这种分析检查是否文档所用的入站适配器中的时间超过 5 秒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-860">Assuming a low latency environment, this analysis checks whether the document spent more than 5 seconds in the inbound adapter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-861">这可能表示通过此主机实例中的入站适配器的消息传输的处理延迟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-861">This may indicate a processing delay in the transport of messages through inbound adapters in this host instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-862">如果此主机实例中存在多个入站的适配器，请考虑将它们分散到其自己的主机，以确定哪个入站的适配器的高延迟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-862">If multiple inbound adapters exist in this host instance, then consider separating them into their own hosts to determine which inbound adapter has high latency.</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-message-delivery-throttling-state-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-870">BizTalk 消息传递限制状态分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-870">BizTalk Message Delivery Throttling State Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-871">BizTalk 消息传递限制状态是之一的限制的主要指示器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-871">The BizTalk message delivery throttling state is one of the primary indicators of throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-872">它是一个标志，指示系统是否限制 （影响 XLANG 消息处理和出站传输协议） 的消息传递。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-872">It is a flag indicating whether the system is throttling message delivery (affecting XLANG message processing and outbound transports).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-873">由计数器的数值表示限制条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-873">The throttling condition is indicated by the numeric value of the counter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-874">下面是值和及其各自的含义的列表：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-874">Here is a list of the values and their respective meaning:</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-messagebox-database-connection-failures-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-893">BizTalk MessageBox 数据库连接故障分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-893">BizTalk MessageBox Database Connection Failures Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-894">此性能计数器是自主机实例启动以来失败的尝试的数据库连接数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-894">This performance counter is the number of attempted database connections that failed since the host instance started.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-895">如果出于任何原因，SQL Server 服务承载 BizTalk 数据库将变得不可用，数据库群集会将资源从活动的计算机传输到被动的计算机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-895">If the SQL Server service hosting the BizTalk databases becomes unavailable for any reason, the database cluster transfers resources from the active computer to the passive computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-896">在此故障转移过程中，BizTalk Server 服务实例会遇到数据库连接失败，这些实例将自动重新启动以重新连接到数据库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-896">During this failover process, the BizTalk Server service instances experience database connection failures and automatically restart to reconnect to the databases.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-897">采用故障转移期间传输的资源后，正在运行的数据库计算机（即前面提到的被动计算机）将开始处理数据库连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-897">The functioning database computer (previously the passive computer) begins processing the database connections after assuming the resources during failover.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-898">当 BizTalk Server 运行时不能与 MessageBox 或管理数据库进行通信时，将发生 DBNetLib （数据库网络库） 错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-898">DBNetLib (Database Network Library) errors occur when the BizTalk Server runtime is unable to communicate with either the MessageBox or management databases.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-899">当发生这种情况时，捕获异常的 BizTalk Server 运行时实例关闭，然后循环每隔一分钟来检查数据库是否可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-899">When this occurs, the BizTalk Server runtime instance that catches the exception shuts down and then cycles every minute to check to see whether the database is available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-900">有关此主题，请参阅引用部分以了解更多信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-900">See the references section for more information on this topic.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-901">当客户端启动到服务器的 TCP/IP 套接字连接时，客户端通常连接到服务器上的特定端口，并请求服务器通过临时（或暂时）TCP 或 UDP 端口进行响应。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-901">When a client initiates a TCP/IP socket connection to a server, the client typically connects to a specific port on the server and requests that the server respond to the client over an ephemeral, or short lived, TCP or UDP port.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-902">在 Windows Server 2003 和 Windows XP，由客户端应用程序使用的临时端口的默认范围是从 1025 到 5000。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-902">On Windows Server 2003 and Windows XP, the default range of ephemeral ports used by client applications is from 1025 through 5000.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-903">在某些情况下，很可能将耗尽默认范围内的可用端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-903">Under certain conditions it is possible that the available ports in the default range will be exhausted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-904">有关此主题，请参阅引用部分以了解更多信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-904">See the references section for more information on this topic.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-905">此分析检查数据库连接失败的任何匹配项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-905">This analysis checks for any occurrence of database connection failures.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-906">数据库连接故障十分重要，因为 BizTalk 无法函数没有数据库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-906">Database connection failures are critical because BizTalk cannot function without the database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-907">如果数据库连接失败的原因是未知的然后请考虑下面列出的引用和/或联系 Microsoft 支持部门确定连接故障的性质。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-907">If the cause of the database connection failure is unknown, then consider the references listed below and/or contact Microsoft Support to determine the nature of the connectivity failure.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-927">6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-927">6</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-928">由于数据库增长而阻止</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-928">Throttling due to database growth</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-929">8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-929">8</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-930">由于会话数过高而阻止</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-930">Throttling due to high session count</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-931">9</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-931">9</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-932">由于线程数过高而阻止</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-932">Throttling due to high thread count</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-933">11</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-933">11</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="84b7a-934">由于发布时的用户替代而阻止</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-934">Throttling due to user override on publishing</span></span>|  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-935">此分析检查其中每个值，并为每个具有特定的警报。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-935">This analysis checks for each of these values and has a specific alert for each of them.</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-orchestrations-resident-in-memory"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-939">BizTalk 业务流程驻留在内存中</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-939">BizTalk Orchestrations Resident in Memory</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-940">当前以主机实例为宿主的业务流程实例的数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-940">Number of orchestration instances currently hosted by the host instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-941">峰值或爆发的业务流程驻留在内存中可能被视为正常，而上升趋势可能表示"积累"在内存中的业务流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-941">While spikes or bursts of orchestrations resident in memory may be considered normal, an increasing trend could indicate a “pile up” of orchestrations in memory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-942">当 BizTalk 无法冻结消息/业务流程实例时，可能会出现随着时间的推移上升趋势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-942">An increasing trend over time may occur when BizTalk is unable to dehydrate messages/orchestration instances.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-943">尝试将此计数器与"XLANG/s Orchestrations(?) 相关联\Dehydratable 业务流程"问号 （？） 所在相同作为此计数器的计数器实例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-943">Try to correlate this counter with “XLANG/s Orchestrations(?)\Dehydratable orchestrations” where the question mark (?) is the same counter instance as this counter.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-944">如果大量的业务流程都驻留在内存中的，并且如果业务流程的数量较少是否可冻结，然后你的业务流程很可能在内存中处于空闲状态，并可能导致内存泄漏情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-944">If a high number of orchestrations are resident in memory and if a low number of orchestrations are dehydratable, then your orchestrations are likely idle in memory and may cause a memory leak condition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-945">如果存在，请选择与"\XLANG/s 业务流程 （*） \Idle 业务流程"相关联时使用此分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-945">Use this analysis in correlation with “\XLANG/s Orchestrations(*)\Idle orchestrations” if present.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-946">在 BizTalk 空闲业务流程中的上升趋势是更好由于冻结业务流程实例的内存泄漏的指标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-946">An increasing trend in BizTalk Idle Orchestrations is a better indicator of memory leaks due to the inability to dehydrate orchestration instances.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-947">此分析检查在驻留在内存和如果超过 50%的驻留在内存中的业务流程不可冻结业务流程中上升趋势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-947">This analysis checks for an increasing trend in orchestrations resident in memory and if more than 50% of the orchestrations resident in memory are not dehydratable.</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-private-bytes-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-953">BizTalk 专用字节分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-953">BizTalk Private Bytes Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-954">这是分配的专用内存的主机实例和类似于"\Process （*） \Private 字节数"性能计数器的兆字节。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-954">This is the megabytes of allocated private memory for the host instance and comparable to the “\Process(*)\Private Bytes” performance counter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-955">专用字节数是内存的当前的大小，以字节为单位的进程已分配不能与其他进程共享。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-955">Private Bytes is the current size, in bytes, of memory that a process has allocated that cannot be shared with other processes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-956">此分析将决定是否任何主机实例消耗的系统内存的大小，并在主机实例是否在内存消耗，随着时间的推移增加。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-956">This analysis determines whether any of the host instances are consuming a large size of the system's memory and whether the host instance is increasing in memory consumption over time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-957">使用大量的内存的主机实例没什么，只要它返回到系统内存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-957">A host instance consuming large portions of memory is fine as long as the it returns the memory to the system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-958">查找增加图表的趋势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-958">Look for increasing trends in the chart.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-959">上升趋势长的一段时间内无法指示内存泄漏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-959">An increasing trend over a long period of time could indicate a memory leak.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-960">此分析检查 10 MB 每小时上升趋势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-960">This analysis checks for a 10 MB-per-hour increasing trend.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-961">可用内存分析和内存泄漏分析与相关联时使用此分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-961">Use this analysis in correlation with the Available Memory analysis and the Memory Leak analysis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-962">此外，请记住，新启动实例将最初显示为内存泄漏时只需正常启动行为的主机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-962">Also, keep in mind that newly started host instances will initially appear as a memory leak when it is simply normal start up behavior.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-963">当进程继续使用内存，以及长的一段时间没有释放内存，内存泄漏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-963">A memory leak is when a process continues to consume memory and not releasing memory over a long period of time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-964">如果你怀疑存在内存泄漏条件，请阅读下面引用"BizTalk 消息的内存增长"中的文章。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-964">If you suspect a memory leak condition, then read the “Memory Growth in BizTalk Messaging” article referenced below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-965">否则为安装并使用调试诊断工具。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-965">Otherwise, install and use the Debug Diag tool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-966">调试诊断工具的详细信息，请参阅引用部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-966">For more information on the Debug Diag Tool, see the references section.</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-virtual-bytes-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-972">BizTalk 虚拟字节分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-972">BizTalk Virtual Bytes Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-973">这是适用于主机实例的虚拟内存保留的兆字节。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-973">This is the megabytes reserved for virtual memory for the host instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-974">此分析将决定是否任何主机实例正在消耗大量的系统内存，且是否随时间推移的内存消耗中增加的主机实例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-974">This analysis determines whether any of the host instances are consuming a large amount of the system's memory and whether the host instance is increasing in memory consumption over time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-975">使用大量的内存的主机实例没什么，只要它返回到系统内存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-975">A host instance consuming large portions of memory is fine as long as it returns the memory to the system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-976">查找增加图表的趋势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-976">Look for increasing trends in the chart.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-977">上升趋势长的一段时间内无法指示内存泄漏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-977">An increasing trend over a long period of time could indicate a memory leak.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-978">此分析检查以虚拟字节为单位按小时 10 MB 的上升趋势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-978">This analysis checks for a 10 MB-per-hour increasing trend in virtual bytes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-979">可用内存分析和内存泄漏分析与相关联时使用此分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-979">Use this analysis in correlation with the Available Memory analysis and the Memory Leak analysis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-980">此外，请记住，新启动实例将最初显示为内存泄漏时只需正常启动行为的主机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-980">Also, keep in mind that newly started host instances will initially appear as a memory leak when it is simply normal start up behavior.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-981">当进程继续使用内存，以及长的一段时间没有释放内存，内存泄漏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-981">A memory leak is when a process continues to consume memory and not releasing memory over a long period of time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-982">如果您怀疑存在内存泄漏条件，然后阅读下面"BizTalk 消息的内存增长"中的文章。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-982">If you suspect a memory leak condition, then read the “Memory Growth in BizTalk Messaging” article below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-983">否则为安装并使用调试诊断工具。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-983">Otherwise, install and use the Debug Diag tool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-984">调试诊断工具的详细信息，请参阅引用部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-984">For more information on the Debug Diag Tool, see the references section.</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-message-agent-database-session-throttling-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-990">BizTalk 消息代理数据库会话限制分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-990">BizTalk Message Agent Database Session Throttling Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-991">这是到 MessageBox 相比限制设置其各自 BizTalk 打开数据库连接数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-991">This is the number of open database connections to the MessageBox compared to its respective BizTalk throttling setting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-992">"数据库连接每个 CPU"是最大并发数据库会话数 （每个 CPU) 限制开始之前允许。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-992">“Database connection per CPU” is the maximum number of concurrent database sessions (per CPU) allowed before throttling begins.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-993">此计数不包括通用的每主机会话池中的空闲数据库会话数，并且只对主机实例实际使用的会话数进行此检查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-993">The idle database sessions in the common per-host session pool do not add to this count, and this check is made strictly on the number of sessions actually being used by the host instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-994">默认情况下，此选项为禁用状态；通常，只有当数据库服务器成为 BizTalk Server 系统的瓶颈时才应启用此设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-994">This option is disabled by default; typically this setting should only be enabled if the database server is a bottleneck in the BizTalk Server system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-995">可以通过使用 BizTalk:Message 代理性能对象类别下的数据库会话性能计数器来监视活动数据库连接数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-995">You can monitor the number of active database connections by using the database session performance counter under the BizTalk:Message Agent performance object category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-996">此参数只影响出站消息阻止功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-996">This parameter only affects outbound message throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-997">输入值 0 可以禁用基于数据库会话数的阻止功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-997">Enter a value of 0 to disable throttling that is based on the number of database sessions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-998">默认值为 0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-998">The default value is 0.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-999">MaxWorkerThreads 注册表项已影响到 BizTalk 可用线程的数目，并可帮助在大部分 BizTalk 的线程都是忙于处理数据库连接的情况下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-999">The MaxWorkerThreads registry key has influence on the number threads available to BizTalk and may help in the case where most of BizTalk’s threads are busy with database connections.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1000">此分析检查到 MessageBox 的打开的数据库连接数是否大于 80%的数据库会话限制，设置，这表明可能限制条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1000">This analysis checks whether the number of open database connections to the MessageBox are greater than 80 percent of the Database Session Throttling setting, indicating a throttling condition is likely.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1004">线程、 DB 会话和限制在[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106793](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106793)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1004">Threads, DB sessions, and throttling at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106793](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=106793)</span></span>  
  
## <a name="biztalk-message-agent-database-session-throttling-threshold-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1005">BizTalk 消息代理数据库会话限制阈值分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1005">BizTalk Message Agent Database Session Throttling Threshold Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1006">这是到 MessageBox 的打开的数据库连接数的当前阈值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1006">This is the current threshold for the number of open database connections to the MessageBox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1007">"数据库连接每个 CPU"是最大并发数据库会话数 （每个 CPU) 限制开始之前允许。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1007">“Database connection per CPU” is the maximum number of concurrent database sessions (per CPU) allowed before throttling begins.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1008">此计数不包括通用的每主机会话池中的空闲数据库会话数，并且只对主机实例实际使用的会话数进行此检查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1008">The idle database sessions in the common per-host session pool do not add to this count, and this check is made strictly on the number of sessions actually being used by the host instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1009">默认情况下，此选项为禁用状态；通常，只有当数据库服务器成为 BizTalk Server 系统的瓶颈时才应启用此设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1009">This option is disabled by default; typically this setting should only be enabled if the database server is a bottleneck in the BizTalk Server system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1010">可以通过使用 BizTalk:Message 代理性能对象类别下的数据库会话性能计数器来监视活动数据库连接数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1010">You can monitor the number of active database connections by using the database session performance counter under the BizTalk:Message Agent performance object category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1011">此参数只影响出站消息阻止功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1011">This parameter only affects outbound message throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1012">输入值 0 可以禁用基于数据库会话数的阻止功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1012">Enter a value of 0 to disable throttling that is based on the number of database sessions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1013">默认值为 0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1013">The default value is 0.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1014">MaxWorkerThreads 注册表项已影响到 BizTalk 可用线程的数目，并可帮助在大部分 BizTalk 的线程都是忙于处理数据库连接的情况下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1014">The MaxWorkerThreads registry key has influence on the number threads available to BizTalk and may help in the case where most of BizTalk’s threads are busy with database connections.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1015">此分析检查此值，以确定是否它进行修改得到了其默认设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1015">This analysis checks this value to see whether it has been modified from its default setting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1016">默认情况下，此设置是 0，表示针对数据库会话限制处于禁用状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1016">By default, this setting is 0, which means throttling on database sessions is disabled.</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-message-agent-in-process-message-count-throttling-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1021">BizTalk 消息代理进程内消息计数限制分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1021">BizTalk Message Agent In-process Message Count Throttling Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1022">这是处理服务类的并发消息数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1022">This is the number of concurrent messages that the service class is processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1023">在主机限制设置的"进程内消息每个 CPU"设置是最大的未处理的消息传递到的终结点管理器 (EPM) 或 XLANG 数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1023">The “In-process messages per CPU” setting in the Host Throttling Settings is the maximum number of messages delivered to the End Point Manager (EPM) or XLANG that have not been processed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1024">这不包括从数据库中检索，但仍在等待中内存中队列的传递的消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1024">This does not include the messages retrieved from the database but still waiting for delivery in the in-memory queue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1025">可以通过使用 BizTalk:Message 代理性能对象类别下的进程内消息计数性能计数器来监视进程内消息数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1025">You can monitor the number of in-process messages by using the In-process message count performance counter under the BizTalk:Message Agent performance object category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1026">此参数提供了阻止机制提示以便您考虑阻止条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1026">This parameter provides a hint to the throttling mechanism for consideration of throttling conditions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1027">实际阈值可能会自我优化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1027">The actual threshold is subject to self-tuning.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1028">通过监视 In-process message count 性能计数器，可以验证实际的阈值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1028">You can verify the actual threshold by monitoring the In-process message count performance counter.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1029">对于大型消息方案 （其中的平均消息大小较高，或消息的处理可能需要大量的消息），此参数可以设置为较小的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1029">For large message scenarios (where either the average message size is high, or the processing of messages may require a large amount of messages), this parameter can be set to a smaller value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1030">如果基于内存的限制过于频繁发生，并且内存阈值获取自动调整为大体上低的值，指示大型消息方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1030">A large message scenario is indicated if memory-based throttling occurs too often and if the memory threshold gets auto-adjusted to a substantially low value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1031">这样将指示出站传输应降低同时处理的消息数以避免占用过高内存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1031">Such behavior would indicate that the outbound transport should process fewer messages concurrently to avoid excessive memory usage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1032">此外，如果适配器一次处理多个消息（例如在向限制并行连接数的服务器发送消息时）可获得更高效率，则可以将此参数优化为低于默认值的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1032">Also, for scenarios where the adapter is more efficient when processing a few messages at a time (for example, when sending to a server that limits concurrent connections), this parameter may be tuned to a lower value than the default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1033">此分析将检查以确定它是否大于 80%的同一名称的其限制设置，它指示限制条件已可能的高的进程内消息 Count 计数器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1033">This analysis checks the High In-Process Message Count counter to determine whether it is greater than 80 percent of its throttling setting under the same name, which indicates a throttling condition is likely.</span></span>

## <a name="biztalkmessage-agent-in-process-message-count-throttling-threshold-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1037">限制阈值分析 BizTalk:Message 代理进程内消息计数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1037">BizTalk:Message Agent In-process Message Count Throttling Threshold Analysis</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1045">对于大型消息方案 （其中的平均消息大小较高，或消息的处理可能需要大量的消息），此参数可以设置为较小的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1045">For large message scenarios (where either the average message size is high, or the processing of messages may require a large amount of messages), this parameter can be set to a smaller value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1046">如果基于内存的限制过于频繁发生，并且内存阈值获取自动调整为大体上低的值，指示大型消息方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1046">A large message scenario is indicated if memory-based throttling occurs too often and if the memory threshold gets auto-adjusted to a substantially low value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1047">这样将指示出站传输应降低同时处理的消息数以避免占用过高内存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1047">Such behavior would indicate that the outbound transport should process fewer messages concurrently to avoid excessive memory usage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1048">此外，如果适配器一次处理多个消息（例如在向限制并行连接数的服务器发送消息时）可获得更高效率，则可以将此参数优化为低于默认值的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1048">Also, for scenarios where the adapter is more efficient when processing a few messages at a time (for example, when sending to a server that limits concurrent connections), this parameter may be tuned to a lower value than the default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1049">此分析检查高进程内消息计数限制为非默认值的阈值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1049">This analysis checks the High In-Process Message Count throttling threshold for a non-default value.</span></span>

## <a name="biztalk-message-agent-process-memory-usage-mb-throttling-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1053">BizTalk 消息代理进程内存使用率 (MB) 限制分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1053">BizTalk Message Agent Process Memory Usage (MB) Throttling Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1054">这是当前进程 (MB) 的内存使用率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1054">This is the memory usage of current process (MB).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1055">BizTalk 进程内存限制可能要发布的批有陡峭的内存需求，或如果线程过多所处理的消息时发生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1055">BizTalk process memory throttling can occur if the batch to be published has steep memory requirements, or if too many threads are processing messages.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1056">如果系统看起来过度限制，请考虑增加主机进程内存使用情况阈值与关联的值，并验证主机实例不会生成"内存不足"错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1056">If the system appears to be over-throttling, consider increasing the value associated with the process memory usage threshold for the host and verify that the host instance does not generate an "out of memory" error.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1057">如果通过增加进程内存使用情况阈值引发"内存不足"错误，请考虑减少内部消息队列大小的值，并且进程内每个 CPU 阈值的消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1057">If an "out of memory" error is raised by increasing the process memory usage threshold, then consider reducing the values for the internal message queue size and in-process messages per CPU thresholds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1058">此策略特别适用于大型消息处理方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1058">This strategy is particularly relevant in large message processing scenarios.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1059">如果你的 BizTalk server 定期运行虚拟内存不足时，请考虑 BizTalk Server 64 位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1059">If your BizTalk server regularly runs out of virtual memory, then consider BizTalk Server 64-bit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1060">在 64 位服务器上的每个进程可以解决最高支持 4 TB 的虚拟内存与在 32 位 2 GB。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1060">Each Process on 64-bit servers can address up to 4 TB’s of virtual memory versus the 2 GB’s in 32-bit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1061">一般情况下，强烈建议 BizTalk 64 位和 64 位 SQL Server。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1061">In general, 64-bit BizTalk and 64-bit SQL Server is highly recommended.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1062">请参阅有关详细信息"BizTalk Server 64 位支持"参考。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1062">See the “BizTalk Server 64-bit Support” reference for more information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1063">此分析检查的进程内存使用量是否大于 80%的具有相同名称的其各自限制阈值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1063">This analysis checks whether the process memory usage is greater than 80 percent of its respective throttling threshold of the same name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1064">默认情况下，BizTalk 进程内存使用情况限制设置是可用于进程的虚拟内存的 25%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1064">By default, the BizTalk Process Memory Usage throttling setting is 25 percent of the virtual memory available to the process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1065">/3GB 开关不起对此设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1065">The /3GB switch has no effect on this setting.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1070">在 BizTalk Server 64 位支持[http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155306](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155306)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1070">BizTalk Server 64-bit Support at [http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155306](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=155306)</span></span>  
  
## <a name="biztalkmessage-agent-process-memory-usage-mb-throttling-threshold-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1071">BizTalk:Message 代理进程内存使用率 (MB) 限制阈值分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1071">BizTalk:Message Agent Process Memory Usage (MB) Throttling Threshold Analysis</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1072">这是当前进程 (MB) 的内存使用量的当前阈值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1072">This is the current threshold for the memory usage of current process (MB).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1073">可能根据实际的此过程，并且其内存消耗模式的可用内存量动态调整阈值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1073">The threshold may be dynamically adjusted depending on the actual amount of memory available to this process and its memory consumption pattern.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1074">BizTalk 进程内存限制可能要发布的批有陡峭的内存需求，或如果线程过多所处理的消息时发生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1074">BizTalk process memory throttling can occur if the batch to be published has steep memory requirements, or if too many threads are processing messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1075">如果系统看起来过度限制，请考虑增加主机进程内存使用情况阈值与关联的值，并验证主机实例不会生成"内存不足"错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1075">If the system appears to be over-throttling, consider increasing the value associated with the process memory usage threshold for the host and verify that the host instance does not generate an "out of memory" error.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1076">如果通过增加进程内存使用情况阈值引发"内存不足"错误，请考虑减少内部消息队列大小的值，并且进程内每个 CPU 阈值的消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1076">If an "out of memory" error is raised by increasing the process memory usage threshold, then consider reducing the values for the internal message queue size and in-process messages per CPU thresholds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1077">此策略特别适用于大型消息处理方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1077">This strategy is particularly relevant in large message processing scenarios.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1078">如果你的 BizTalk server 定期运行虚拟内存不足时，请考虑 BizTalk Server 64 位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1078">If your BizTalk server regularly runs out of virtual memory, then consider BizTalk Server 64-bit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1079">在 64 位服务器上的每个进程可以解决最高支持 4 TB 的虚拟内存与在 32 位 2 GB。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1079">Each Process on 64-bit servers can address up to 4 TB’s of virtual memory versus the 2 GB’s in 32-bit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1080">一般情况下，强烈建议 BizTalk 64 位和 64 位 SQL Server。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1080">In general, 64-bit BizTalk and 64-bit SQL Server is highly recommended.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1081">请参阅有关详细信息"BizTalk Server 64 位支持"参考。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1081">See the “BizTalk Server 64-bit Support” reference for more information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84b7a-1082">此分析检查是否将进程内存限制设置为非默认值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84b7a-1082">This analysis checks whether the Process memory throttling is set to a non-default value.</span></span>
